1934.12.31

Zhenyuan City Has Been Reported Recovered, Bandits Fled Westward from Shibing and Huangping, Part Fleeing to Yuqing and Shiqian, Various Armies Blocking and Pursuing Separately 1

(Changsha) Zhou Hunyuan's troops rushed to Zhenyuan and, joining Wu Qiwai's army, engaged in fierce battles with the pseudo 13th and 2nd Army Corps. Over a thousand bandits were killed, and Zhenyuan City was recovered at dusk on the 27th. A portion of the bandits fled westward towards Lushan via Shibing and Huangping, while another portion fled northwest towards Yuqing and Shiqian. The Qian army and You army are both stationed in the Lushan area to prevent bandits from infiltrating internally. Liu and Xue's various units are pursuing and blocking them along different routes. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Military News: Wang Jialie's troops and the Central Army's subordinate units recaptured Zhenyuan on the afternoon of the 28th. The bandits fled towards the Shiqian and Yinjiang areas. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

◎ Guiyang The Central Army and Qian Army's Cai Brigade recaptured Zhenyuan on the afternoon of the 28th, with numerous captures and killings. The bandits fled towards the Shiqian and Yinjiang areas. Furthermore, a portion of the bandits fled across Huangping and Yuqing, fleeing towards Longxi. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

◎ Guiyang After being defeated on the 28th, the bandits defended Zhenxiong Pass, but were subsequently defeated by Xue Yue's troops. On the 29th, the Central Army, with Wu's column, launched a fierce attack from Zhenyuan towards the Shibing-Huangping line. Zhou's column launched an attack and suppression against the bandits in Huangping via Sansui, through the Shidongkou, Wenggu, and Long area, with the hope of achieving a pincer attack in conjunction with the Qian Army. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Chongqing) Yang Sen and Li Jiayu have both telegraphed Liu Xiang, reorganizing their armies and awaiting orders for a general offensive against the bandits. Furthermore, Yang Sen has scheduled a grand review of the troops stationed in Shunqing and the volunteer army and student army, along with demonstrations of national martial arts, horse racing competitions, and soccer matches on New Year's Day at the Tumen Temple Grand Training Ground outside the South Gate of Shunqing. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Wan Fulin's Troops Enter the Mountains to Search for Liu's Bandits; Bandits Already Trapped in the Core; Tong County Temporarily Under Martial Law 2

(Beiping) The remnants of Liu Guitang's bandits in the Mentougou, Mayu Village, and Dahui Field areas have been routed towards Qitang and Yanchi and other places as a result of suppression efforts by Wan Fulin's troops. These areas have now been surrounded by Tang's troops. The bandits are hiding in various mountain valleys. At dawn today, the battalion sent teams into the mountains to search and has trapped the bandits in the core. Due to the bandits carrying a large number of internal tickets, it is inconvenient to launch a fierce attack, so they are simply being surrounded and a solution is being sought gradually. It is reported that when the bandits fled from Yixian, Fangshan, and other places, they looted along the way, leaving ten houses empty out of every ten. According to intelligence, the bandits plan to flee to Changping, attempting to join the small contingent of Yang Hou, who is plotting a mutiny in the Shangdu area, along the Ping-Sui Railway line. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Tong County reports by telephone that after the remnants of Liu's bandits once again disrupted the war zone, they were intercepted by local militia and police along the way, and small groups of three to five bandits are roaming in various townships, disturbing the local area. Tong County, in order to prevent scattered bandits from entering the city, has imposed temporary martial law starting from the 29th, with the garrison troops and the county Public Security Bureau responsible for security. Entrances and exits at all city gates are subject to strict inspection, and nighttime patrols are especially strict. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Near Dongshimen in Tong County, over two hundred remnants of Liu Guitang's troops have been discovered. The 32nd Army has dispatched troops to block and attack them. They have now fled towards the Sanhe and Bindi areas. Upon receiving the report, the Hebei Provincial Government has ordered the security teams and defense corps of these two counties and neighboring counties to implement strict prevention and blockade measures to prevent them from flowing into the war zone. Two hundred members of Liu's bandits are currently surrounded in the mountains around Qitang near Pingxi Mentougou, and the military and police are strictly preventing them from fleeing elsewhere. (30th Special Dispatch)

War Zone Clearance Committee Scheduled to Hold Regular Meeting 3

(Beiping) The War Zone Clearance Committee is scheduled to hold a regular meeting on January 4th of next year. Yin Tong traveled to Tianjin today to participate in the New Year's Day group worship of the Beijing-Shanhaiguan Railway Bureau staff. (30th Special Dispatch)

Northeast Postal Service News 4

(Beiping) Postal service to the Northeast is scheduled to resume receiving mail from January 10th. Parcel and remittance services will be handled from February 1st. The relay organization passing through a certain point in Yugu Beikou will transfer mail entering the pass and will use special postage stamps. Those who mistakenly affix other types of invalid postage stamps will be responsible for paying the deficiency by the relay organization and will not collect the arrears from the recipient. (30th Special Dispatch)

Japan Announces Treaty Abolition; No Immediate Impact; Expansion of Armaments by Various Countries is an Inevitable Trend 5

(Nanjing) Regarding Japan's announcement of the abolition of the Washington Naval Treaty, a reporter inquired on the 30th with a senior official familiar with the diplomatic situation. According to him, although Japan has now announced the abandonment of the naval treaty, it will not take effect until after December 31, 1936. There will be no significant impact in these two years. However, the secret expansion of armaments by various countries is an inevitable trend. If a new agreement can be generated in the future to replace the treaty, it will naturally continue to maintain the current peaceful situation. Otherwise, not only will naval disarmament be affected, but general disarmament will also suffer adversely. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Soviet Russian Returnee Discusses the Situation of Russo-Japanese Preparations for War; Difficult to Erupt Immediately 6

(Nanjing) A gentleman who returned from Russia said, regarding the atmosphere of Russo-Japanese war, from a superficial observation, there is a possibility of war between the two sides. But in reality, Japan's land and sea defenses in the three northeastern provinces have not been completed, and Russia's heavy industry also needs to continue its efforts, which cannot be arranged in a short period of time. It is too early to talk about war at this time. The tense situation on the borders of the two countries proves the danger of both sides fearing war. According to what the Russians have passed down, Japan's plan for dealing with the war with Russia is to adopt an elliptical folding fan shape, using Xinjiang as a base for cutting off the land army connection between Russia. Inner Mongolia is used as a base for cutting off the connection between Outer Mongolia and Russia. The center of military command focuses on the northern route, while the main force is in the central route. Negotiations between Russia and Japan on the eastern railway have been going on for a long time. On the surface, it is due to issues such as price and retirement pay for Russian employees. In fact, it is a means of suppressing war. The Japanese could have seized the entire Eastern Railway's business rights without spending a penny, but they were afraid that the war would break out quickly, which would be unfavorable to them. Therefore, on the surface, they used a buying and selling policy to ease the Russian atmosphere, while in reality, they intensified military preparations. The Russians also knew the Japanese methods, but because their own heavy industry had not yet been completed, they also took the same approach, dealing with each other with duplicity. Since the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and the Soviet Union, commercial friendship has been increasing day by day. They have the greatest hope for the future of China's revitalization, and they hope that China can have far-reaching plans so that there are no barriers between the two countries. As for all other issues, as long as China itself has a solution, the solution will not be a problem. The Soviet Union's construction focuses on heavy industry, and it employs more than 1,000 foreign technicians who are distributed in various industrial areas to provide guidance. Collective systems are emphasized for factory construction and the people's clothing, food, housing, and transportation. The largest factories often have more than 100,000 workers, and the smallest factories also have thousands of workers. The buildings are all large Western-style houses with dozens of floors. Small family-style Western houses like those in China are not often seen. The rate of political decision-making is very high. The most important official business can be completed in a few tens of minutes, and less important matters cannot exceed one day. Otherwise, the person in charge will be severely punished. (30th Special Dispatch)

Sun Ke Passes Through Jinan to Go North 7

(Beiping) Sun Ke passed through Jinan to go to Beijing. Han Fuju met him at the station. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Sun Ke took a special train north from Nanjing last night and is expected to arrive in Beijing tomorrow morning to inspect the situation in North China and welcome his wife back to Beijing. Sun will stay in Beijing for about a week and must rush back to Nanjing before January 14 to preside over the swearing-in ceremony for the newly appointed legislators. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) Sun Ke boarded the Taishan special train at 6:00 AM on the 30th and attached it to the Jinpu express train, passing through Xuzhou from Nanjing to Beijing. Shao Lizi arrived in Xuzhou from Nanjing on the morning of the 30th and immediately transferred to a train west to return to Shaanxi. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Sun Ke is scheduled to pass through Tianjin at 4:20 AM on the 31st to visit his wife, who is receiving treatment at the Xiehe Hospital. (30th Special Dispatch)

Zhejiang New Games Preparations; Welcome Chairman Chiang; Kong Xiangxi Talks in Hangzhou; Yang Yongtai and Ou Fangpu Arrive in Hangzhou 8

(Hangzhou) The Zhejiang New Games Promotion Association is scheduled to hold a welcoming conference for Chairman Chiang at the Provincial Party Headquarters Auditorium on the morning of the 31st and invite Chiang to give instructions. Those participating in the welcome must enter with a ticket. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Kong Xiangxi met with reporters at 11:30 PM on the 29th and said that the rumors about the silver issue have subsided since the Ministry of Finance strictly prohibited the spreading of rumors. The Ministry of Finance has now organized a balance committee to handle parity matters by the Central, China, and Communications Banks, so the current exchange rate has stabilized. In order to understand the economic situation of various provinces and regions, he had previously visited various places in North and Central China, so he also plans to visit South China, but the travel date is undecided. Wang Liangchou came to Hangzhou with Chairman Chiang, and it is also undecided whether he will travel south again. Also, regarding the Zhejiang Provincial Finance's shortfall, he said that the Ministry of Finance can find ways to subsidize it. The Finance Department Director Xu Qingfu has already submitted the drafted Zhejiang Financial Brief to Kong for review on the 30th. Kong returned to Shanghai on the afternoon of the 30th and will come to Hangzhou again to participate in the opening ceremony of the new Central Bank of Hangzhou building on January 3rd. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Wang Longhui took a fast train to Shanghai at 2:00 PM today. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Kong Xiangxi went to Shanghai and then to Beijing at 5:50 PM today. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Chu Minyi and Yang Yongtai arrived in Hangzhou at 12:30 PM today. Huang Shao Xiong and Huang Hua Biao greeted them at the station. Chu and Yang are currently staying at the Xileng Hotel. Zhang Jingjiang, Ye Chu Cang, and Qian Xin Zhi arrived in Hangzhou from Shanghai at 7:30 PM tonight and are staying at the Xinxin Hotel. Ou Fangpu also arrived here today. The newly appointed members of the Zhejiang Provincial Government are scheduled to be sworn in at 9:00 AM on New Year's Day, with Chu Minyi presiding over the oath. (30th Special Dispatch)

Western Sailors Strike in Hong Kong; Mediation Fails 9

(Hong Kong) Western sailors went on strike at 12:00 AM on the 29th. Many inland river steamers were suspended as a result. Relevant parties ran around to mediate but failed. Labor and management are still deadlocked. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) After convening a general meeting of members, the Chinese Seamen's Union and the Chinese Marine Engineers' Association issued an ultimatum today to the shipowner of the Yutong ship (transliteration), demanding that the four senior British crew members who were recently dismissed be reinstated. Otherwise, all six hundred European crew members of river and sea ships will go on strike. The situation is quite tense now. If the demand is not met, the most severe labor unrest in Hong Kong's industry will occur, and Hong Kong's trade will be suspended. This ultimatum expires at midnight on Tuesday. It is expected that the shipowner will exert pressure to prevent the strike, but the two unions are confident that if the four dismissed crew members are not reinstated, the number of those joining the strike will be as many as six hundred. It was found that the two unions decided to strike last night. Those affected include 13 river boats and 40 British crew members. (30th Reuters Dispatch)

He Guoguang Leads the General Headquarters Staff Corps to Arrive in Hankou; Scheduled to Go to Yichang on the 3rd to Enter Sichuan to Be Responsible for Planning the Military Suppression of Bandits 10

(Hankou) He Guoguang, at 2:00 PM on the 30th, led the majority of the General Headquarters Staff Corps personnel, arriving in Hankou from Xun by the Fuyang steamer. Various military and political dignitaries welcomed them grandly. He checked into the Yangtze River Hotel and is scheduled to go to Yichang on the 3rd to enter Sichuan. He stated that the Staff Corps is a special agency organized by the Chairman's General Headquarters, which will be established in Chongqing and will be responsible for planning the military suppression of bandits, as well as supervising and commanding. Its orders will be issued in the name of the Chairman and countersigned by Liu Xiang. He and others are scheduled to take the original ship to Yichang on the 3rd, waiting for Kang Ze, the Director of the Political Training Department, to enter Sichuan together. After arriving in Sichuan, they will first inspect the front lines. As for the Jiangxi bandits, they have been largely suppressed. The Jiangxi General Headquarters has decided to be abolished. It will not receive official documents next month, and it can be concluded by the end of the month. Zhang Xueliang and He Chengjun hosted a dinner for He, during which there were discussions. It is rumored that the Sichuan Provincial Government can be established next month. The Central Government will send Zhang Qun, and Chiang will send He Chengjun to preside over the oath. (31st Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) The General Headquarters Staff Corps personnel arrived in Hankou on the 30th, totaling 700 people. None of them disembarked. Deputy Director Yang Jihui was originally in Sichuan. Liu Yiren, the director of the first section, and Wang Youyong, the director of the second section, are in Shanghai. Kang Ze, the Director of the Political Training Department, is in Xingzi County and will come to Hankou to gather and enter Sichuan. The staff of the Political Department and the personnel sent to various armies to handle political training total 360 people. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Nanchang) The Jiujiang telephone reported at 9:00 AM on the 30th that He Guoguang and the Staff Corps special train arrived in Xun at 5:30 PM on the 29th. Leaders from all walks of life and mass organizations all went to the station to welcome them and presented a "Ten Thousand People Umbrella" as a souvenir. In the evening, they attended a banquet hosted by the outside world. At 1:00 AM on the 30th, they boarded a special steamer westward. Mass representatives gathered on the riverbank to see them off. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hankou) The General Headquarters Staff Corps, a group of more than 200 people, led by the Corps Director He Guoguang, arrived in Hankou from Xun by the Fuyang steamer at 3:00 PM on the 30th. Those who went to the pier in Wuhan to welcome them included He Chengjun, Xu Yuanquan, Ye Peng, Tang Guozhen, Cao Zhenwu, Chen Xizeng, and Qiu Jia and other representatives of various Sichuan troops. After disembarking, He went to the Yangtze River Hotel to rest and met with the welcoming personnel. He is scheduled to take the original ship to Yichang on January 3rd and change ships to enter Sichuan. All the people who came with him did not disembark and stayed on the Fuyang steamer awaiting orders to go west. According to He's words to reporters, the Staff Corps will be stationed in Chongqing. Whether he will go to the front for inspection will be determined after arriving in Chongqing. The nature of the Staff Corps is a special agency established by the Chairman to supervise and guide the suppression of bandits. In the future, the orders for the suppression of bandits will be drafted by the Staff Corps, issued in the name of the Chairman and countersigned by Liu, the Commander-in-Chief, and Xiang, the Deputy Commander. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Total National Grain Reserves 11

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior's general inspection of national warehouses has been completed by the provinces. The total national grain reserves are estimated to be over 4 million shi. The Ministry of Interior has issued orders to properly store the reserves and ordered the warehouses in various places to be thoroughly organized to ensure the people's food supply. (30th Special Dispatch)

Guan Suru and Others Arrive in Beijing; According to Them, This Trip is for Sightseeing and Has No Mission 12

(Beiping) Guangdong Central Committee member Guan Suru and Li Qi'an arrived in Beijing this morning. According to them, because they have been in the south for a long time, they are taking a New Year's holiday after attending the Fifth Plenary Session to visit friends in Beijing and visit scenic spots and have no mission. When he was in Nanjing, he visited Chiang, but because Chiang was suffering from toothache, he could not talk much. Hu is currently in Hong Kong, and he has not recently received any letters or telegrams from him. Hu's entry into Beijing was negotiated by Wang Liangchou, but the results are unknown. The Southwest and the Central Government are originally cooperating, and now they are discussing practical measures. The Southwest's dispatch of personnel to be stationed in Beijing and the establishment of an office there are only seen in newspaper reports. There is no such preparation, nor is it necessary. As for the abolition of the two agencies, he is not yet aware. Ou Fangpu came north to attend the Fifth Plenary Session, but due to the delay in waiting for a boat, he failed to arrive in time to participate. He has now gone to Hangzhou to visit Chiang and Kong to discuss financial issues and measures for the Guangdong army to pursue and suppress the remaining bandits. After the remaining bandits in Jiangxi fled to the border of Guangdong and Guangxi, they suffered heavy losses due to the strict blockade, with approximately 10,000 casualties and injuries. Many guns were seized. The remaining bandits have now fled to the border of Guizhou. They plan to stay in Beijing for about four or five days, visit Huang and visit various scenic spots before returning to Nanjing. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Guan Suru and Li Qi'an arrived in Beijing at 8:00 AM on the 30th. According to Guan, they came to Beijing to visit friends and visit scenic spots and will return to Nanjing in four or five days. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Beijing City Salt District Decides to Open on New Year's Day 13

Limited to Fine Salt, Huainan, and Huaibei Salt Merchants

(Nanjing) The opening date for the salt district in this city has been decided as New Year's Day. The Salt Affairs Administration has ordered the Huaibei Salt Transport Envoy Office, the Huainan Deputy Office, and the Xiaguan Inspection Bureau to instruct the salt merchants to comply. This opening is not the entire Jiangpu six salt bank, but the Beijing city area carved out of the salt bank and is limited to three types of salt merchants: fine salt, Huainan, and Huaibei. Not all salt merchants across the country can freely sell in Beijing. Therefore, the name is the free salt district of Huainan, Huaibei, and Jing salt carved out of the six salt banks of Jiangpu with restrictions in Beijing city. From now on, any merchant can transport and sell Huainan salt to Beijing. There were originally 13 fine salt companies in the country. In addition to the six Yingkou companies that have been banned from selling, there are also seven companies, including Jiuda, Yongyu, Tongyi, Wuhe, Minsheng, and Dingyi. Among them, the former four are setting up distribution offices in Xiaguan, and they will simultaneously enter the city for business at that time. Fine salt is all packaged, with each package weighing thirteen taels and six qian. In recent years, business has declined, and most have reduced the weight to increase revenue. In order to eliminate malpractices, the authorities decided to rectify the package weight in addition to opening up the city. All Huai salt and fine salt imports must be weighed, calculated at 100 catties per load according to the market scale. As for the selling price, it will be according to the original price without increasing or decreasing. The current cost of each load of salt is about two yuan, plus a registration fee of more than seven yuan per load, totaling about more than nine yuan, so the price per catty is about nine to ten cents. (30th Special Dispatch)

Salt Administration Reform Committee Under Preparation Scheduled to be Established on January 20th 14

(Nanjing) The Salt Administration Reform Committee is under preparation. The committee will have seven to nine members, with the Premier of the Executive Yuan, Wang, as the chairman, and the Minister of Finance, Kong, and the Minister of Industry, Chen, as ex officio members. The selection of the remaining committee members has been decided in principle. All current salt administration officials or coarse and fine salt merchants cannot participate. It has been roughly determined that there are about four or five people. After being submitted by the Executive Yuan to the Central Political Conference for discussion and resolution, they will take on their respective responsibilities. The committee is scheduled to be established on January 20th to begin studying and organizing measures such as field production. If necessary, the competent authorities will be invited to attend and explain. (30th Special Dispatch)

Heads of the Jixian Poor People's Association Escorted to the Commissioner's Office for Interrogation 15

(Beiping) After the arrest and interrogation of more than seventy leaders of the Jixian Poor People's Association, eleven of them are considered important. The Jixian government sent police to escort them to the Tong County Commissioner's Office for interrogation this afternoon. (30th Special Dispatch)

Zhang Qun Inspects Dingxian 16

(Tianjin) Hubei Chairman Zhang Qun arrived in Dingxian at 6:00 AM on the 29th. Yan Yangchu and Dingxian County Chief Lu Fu led the gentry of the entire county to welcome him. At 9:00 AM that day, he visited the Pingjiao Association and the Research Institute. In the afternoon, he went to the countryside to visit the Xiaochen Village Model Rural Area. On the 30th, he visited the agricultural field and health center in the city. In the afternoon, he gave a speech at the Pingjiao Association. At 6:00 AM on the 31st, he took a fast train back to Hankou. (30th Special Dispatch)

Yutian Militia Dispute; Yin Rugeng Visits Tianjin to Discuss with Japanese Consul 17

(Tianjin) The Yutian Second District Militia, totaling over two hundred men, are under the jurisdiction of Wang Bingxiao. The militiamen are recruited from various villages. The original regulations stipulated a monthly salary of eight yuan per person, with food expenses shared by the villages. When the salary was issued on the 28th, due to insufficient funds, only five yuan was issued per person, deducting three yuan for food expenses. The militiamen refused to accept this and gathered to make a public disturbance. That night, sixty men mutinied and were surrounded and disarmed by Wang Bingxiao's troops. However, the remaining men are also unstable. On the 29th, they formed a confrontational situation with the militia of Ya Hongqiao. The security team took the opportunity to agitate, and the situation is very bad. The gentry of various villages are currently trying their best to mediate. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Yutian Security Team is becoming increasingly rampant. Each company commander occupies a defensive area, acts freely, and levies supplies from villagers. The first battalion commander, Sun Yucheng, the second company commander, Wang Ziming, and the third company commander, Shi Zhensheng, are extremely domineering. On the 28th, because Zhang Xiaoxuan's father and son, residents of Dananzhuang in the eighth district of the defense area, were extremely poor and unable to pay the donation, the team sent more than ten soldiers to arrest them in the middle of the night. All three of the father and sons were shot and killed. Zhang's daughter-in-law, filled with grief and indignation, committed suicide by hanging. The whole family died tragically. After this incident occurred, more and more villagers fled in fear of disaster. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) At 10:00 AM this morning, Yin Rugeng visited the Japanese Consul in Tianjin, Kawagoe Shigeru, and senior staff officers of the Japanese army stationed in North China, Oki and Kawaguchi, to discuss the deployment of the security supplementary team in the Yutian war zone for reorganization and the planned location of the new defense area. Zhu Shiqin was originally scheduled to arrive in Tianjin this afternoon to assist Yin in discussing with the Japanese side, but the matter was changed to a night train to Tianjin and will go to Yutian on the 31st. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng went to Tianjin yesterday to report important matters to Yu Xuezhong. After completing the official business, he returned to Beijing tonight. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) At 7:20 PM this afternoon, Yin Tong returned to Tianjin from Beijing. Yin Rugeng completed negotiations with the Japanese side on the Yutian issue in Tianjin and returned to Beijing at 4:00 PM this afternoon. (30th Special Dispatch)

Yang's Bandits Disrupt Zhongyixian; Martial Law Declared 18

(Tianjin) Yang Hou Xiaozi's bandits, who are disrupting Yixian, have been pursued by the militia of Fuping, Pingshan, and Quyang counties. They once tried to escape into the war zone but were intercepted by the first general detachment of the war zone security forces. On the 27th, they fled back to Yixian and occupied Zhangfang Town, cutting off telephone lines. The county chief sent militia and police to suppress them. On the 28th, the bandits, upon hearing the news, fled through Shimen, Siganchi, Wajing, Tian, and the various villages of Yangtougang, Eighteen Acres of Land, Xinkaikou, and Xishifu, and other places, and fled to the Houfuying area on the border of Yixian and Mancheng. In the more than sixty villages they passed, all the property was looted, and countless men and women held for ransom were killed. More than two hundred people were kidnapped. On the morning of the 29th, they engaged in a fierce battle with the Yishui militia in Houfuying. Yixian has declared martial law, the four gates are tightly closed, and the militia are all reinforced to go. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Yang Hou Xiaozi's bandits are currently entrenched in the area where Yixian, Mancheng, and Wanxian meet. This area is located in the deep mountains of Weizhuang, Fengjialing, and Qiniangzhai villages, which is very strategically advantageous and has inconvenient transportation. The bandits are entrenched in the mountains, with a part of them harassing in all directions, forcing farmers to join their ranks, and kidnapping women, all of whom are raped. Male hostages who do not send ransom money are poured with kerosene into their mouths and burned to death. Many have died tragically. All the villagers' militia guns have been confiscated by the bandits. They are currently gathering a group of more than seven or eight hundred people, making it difficult to suppress them. (30th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Because Yang Hou Xiao bandits are disrupting the border between Yixian and Mancheng, and are only sixty li away from Baoding, the Baoding headquarters dispatched a battalion of infantry on the 30th to rush to assist the militia in suppressing them. (30th Special Dispatch)

Wuhan Holds General Inspection of New Life Movement 19

(Hankou) The Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau held a general inspection of the New Life Movement, which was completed today. A total of 236,000 people received guidance, mostly from the business community. The city appearance has been improved. (30th Special Dispatch)

Current Affairs Commentary

A Review of Global Economic Trends in the Past Year (Part 2) by Tong 20

Amidst the global economic downturn, Japan's economic situation alone is gradually improving. Its courage to move forward has caused unease and resistance among various countries. Japan's industrial economy has four major pillars: (1) rice, (2) silk cocoons, (3) export industries, and (4) military industries. Except for rice and silk cocoons, which have become pressing rural problems due to last year's bumper harvest and the drop in the U.S. raw silk market, the export and military industries are experiencing rapid development. In terms of rice production in rural areas, it exceeded 70 million *koku* in 1933. In addition, Korea and Taiwan produced over 20 million *koku* of rice, making it a rare bumper year for Japan. As a result, rice prices fell excessively, and the government is striving for rice control and adjustment of rice from overseas territories. The main purpose of the Rice Control Law is to consider both the cost of rice production and the livelihood of the people, and to determine the highest and lowest rice prices every December. Based on these prices, rice is bought and sold. On December 16, 1933, the Rice Control Committee decided that the highest price would be 30 yen and 50 sen, and the lowest price would be 23 yen and 30 sen. To date, the government's expenditure on rice purchased has exceeded 500 million yen.

Although rice prices have risen daily since the government's purchases, some rural areas still face food shortages due to the bumper harvest. For example, farmers in Niigata Prefecture appealed to the government at the end of April this year for the allocation of old rice stocks for relief due to rice shortages. Moreover, many farmers in remote rural areas grow rice but cannot afford to eat it. This is mainly due to improper distribution.

Silkworm cocoons are the second most important product for Japanese farming households. However, in the past year, the sluggish raw silk market has led to extremely low prices. In the spring of 1933, silk prices rose to 1,000 yen, but by the turn of summer and autumn, they plummeted to half the value of 500 yen. This was because Roosevelt's New Deal revival movement was initially vigorous but faltered after summer. Japan's raw silk exports account for more than 80% of its total output, and most of it is exported to the United States. Therefore, Japanese products account for 95% of the raw silk consumed in the United States. The state of the Japanese silk cocoon market depends entirely on the prosperity or decline of the American market. According to the National Textile Association of America, the consumption of raw silk in the year from July 1933 to June 1934 was 440,000 bales, the lowest consumption since 1925. In recent years, the widespread sale of rayon has also greatly developed this industry, posing a significant threat to the future of Japanese raw silk.

Japan's export industries have indeed experienced rapid growth. The fundamental reason for this is that Japan's machinery industry seized the opportunity when European countries were preoccupied with the European War and made great strides. It broke away from the era of imitating Europe and America and entered an organization of original production. At the same time, it strived to rationalize production, making management methods more rigorous, and meticulously studied technological progress to ensure excellent product quality and low costs, in order to complete its dumping policy. As a result of expanding old markets and developing new markets in recent years, Japanese goods had an export value of 1.861 billion yen in 1933, an increase of 62.3% compared to 1931. By May of this year, the cumulative amount was approximately 820 million yen, an increase of 22.9% compared to the same period last year.

In addition, in the Far East, Soviet Russia recently announced that it would abolish the rationing system from January 1, 1935. Amidst the approaching end of the year, this move by Soviet Russia adds new data to the world's economic history. Since 1929, Soviet Russia has implemented a rationing system as part of its Five-Year Plan. All people had to buy bread and other daily necessities with ration tickets. On November 28 of this year, the Central Committee of the Communist Party passed a resolution applying to the Council of People's Commissars to abolish this system. Chairman Molotov of the Council of People's Commissars also reported to the meeting that this measure would stimulate the progress of agriculture and industry, reduce market prices, and increase workers' wages, in order to consolidate the ruble and develop trade. The plenary session adopted seven other measures. From the plans formulated, it can be seen that the Soviet Russian economy will return to the New Economic Policy of 1921 and gradually tend toward a capitalist structure. This point is a unique change in the world economy in 1934. How the world economy will change in the future, how can we predict?

US Navy to Conduct Unprecedented Maneuvers Next Summer Concurrent with Japan's Treaty Abandonment Announcement; Clearly of Great Significance; 177 Warships and Over 500 Aircraft to Participate; Maneuver Area Covers 5 Million Square Miles Throughout the Eastern Pacific 21

◎San Pedro, California: Japan announced the abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty today. Simultaneously, U.S. Navy Fleet Commander Admiral Reeves released an unprecedented plan for U.S. naval maneuvers in the Pacific. The exercises, scheduled from May 3 to June 10 next summer, will cover approximately 5 million square miles throughout the Eastern Pacific, nearly reaching the Eastern Sea. The fleet assembled at sea under a single commander will be the most formidable in world naval history. A total of 177 warships will participate, along with 577 naval aircraft, the naval airship Macon, and four aircraft carriers. The naval officers, men and operators will total 55,000. The fleet will be divided into three parts, based at Honolulu, the Aleutian Islands, and Midway Island in the North Pacific. (Reuters, 29th)

◎St. Paul, USA: U.S. Fleet Commander Admiral Reeves announced today that the U.S. fleet will conduct its largest naval exercise in history next summer. The exercise area will be in the North Pacific, extending from the Aleutian Islands in the north to Midway Island in the south, and reaching the Californian coast in the east. Reeves mentioned that the U.S. fleet may sail to Wake Island, which is closer to Japan than the United States, but he did not explicitly state this. Wake Island is located approximately midway between the Hawaiian Islands and Japan. In April next year, the fleet will concentrate in Los Angeles, San Diego, San Francisco, and Puget Sound. The exercise period will last for several months. The Patrol Force originally stationed along the Atlantic coast will also pass through the Panama Canal in mid-March to participate. The timing of Reeves' announcement, coinciding with Japan's notification of treaty abrogation, is considered very significant. Participating in the exercise will be battleships, cruisers, destroyers, torpedo boat destroyers, torpedo boats, and

other auxiliary warships, totaling 177 vessels, 577 aircraft, and the large airship Macon. Midway Island, northwest of the Hawaiian Islands, will serve as the forward base for the fleet. During the exercise, battleships will sail west to Wake Island. Some ships of the Asiatic Fleet may meet the battle fleet and patrol fleet in the central Pacific. Reeves also stated that during the exercise, the U.S. fleet will be divided into three groups. The Southern Fleet will advance westward from San Diego and San Pedro to Pearl Harbor in the Hawaiian Islands, while the Northern Fleet will secretly proceed from the Aleutian Islands to the secret naval port that the naval air force has quietly established in recent years. The main fleet will also dispatch repair ships, fuel ships, and transport ships to Midway Island before the fleet departs from the mainland.

Prior to sailing along the coast, there will be practice firing and other activities. (National News Agency, 29th)

Japan's Treaty Abrogation is a Retrogressive Act Threatening World Peace; Its Impact Concerns All Treaties Related to the Far East; The Key to the Situation Lies in Britain's Hands 22

(Washington) American figures believe that Japan's declaration of treaty abrogation will have a profound impact on world peace. From now on, naval and commercial competition in the United States, the Far East, South America, and other areas of the Pacific will intensify. The entire relationship between Britain and the United States will also be called into question. While the fundamental rapprochement between Britain and the United States due to Japan is possible, the dream of a united Anglo-Saxon race, at least in spirit, may be shattered. This is because the U.S. Navy wants to maintain its superiority over Japan while maintaining equality with Britain. However, Britain intends to have a navy capable of resisting the combined forces of the two major European naval powers. Italy wants to maintain a navy equal to that of France, while France wants its navy to be able to resist the combined navies of Italy and Germany. The naval competition between France and Italy compels Britain to build new ships, which in turn triggers competition between Britain and the United States. The reason why the dream of Anglo-Saxon unity may not be realized lies here. Moreover, the U.S. government believes that the Washington Naval Treaty stipulated that Britain and the United States maintain the status quo in certain territories or dependencies in the Pacific and not add new defensive works (Washington Naval Treaty, Article 19) because Japan recognized the 5:5:3 ratio. Now that Japan has declared the abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty and no longer recognizes the existing ratio, the provision prohibiting the addition of defensive works in the Pacific dependencies naturally loses its effect. At the same time, the Nine-Power Treaty guaranteeing the Open Door Policy in China and the Four-Power Treaty guaranteeing the territories of the signatory countries in the Far East will also lose their effect due to the abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty. (Note: The Four-Power Treaty was signed simultaneously with the Washington Naval Treaty and the Nine-Power Treaty. The signatories were Britain, the United States, France, and Japan. Its main purpose was to maintain general peace and maintain and respect the rights of each country in all islands and territories in the Pacific, replacing the Anglo-Japanese Alliance.) In addition, the Dutch East Indies occupy a very important strategic position. Since the Washington Treaties have become invalid, there is no protection. People are quite worried about Japan's future intentions toward the island. Now the key to the situation undoubtedly lies in Britain's hands. Americans hope that Britain and the United States can negotiate, even if they cannot conclude an alliance, they can also closely cooperate due to Japan in order to resist Japan in future naval conferences. However, the United States deeply fears that Britain will eventually abandon the Open Door Policy in China in exchange for commercial interests in Manchuria, and that Britain will express sympathy with Japan on naval issues, disregarding the opinions of the United States and deciding to increase the number of British light cruisers. The United States' modification of the principle of freedom of the seas is mostly to please Britain. As for establishing friendly relations with Soviet Russia, preparing to open the new Nicaragua Canal, and preparing to establish naval and air force bases along the coast of Alaska, these are to resist Japan's power in the Far East. (Havas, 29th)

Notifying the Abrogation; Saito Issues a Declaration Hypocritically Expressing Goodwill Towards the United States; Naval Stance Remains Unchanged 23

(Washington) Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito entered the State Department today to formally present U.S. Secretary of State Hull with a written notification that Japan is abrogating the Washington Naval Treaty and will no longer be bound by the treaty after December 31, 1936. He stated that Japan's abrogation of the treaty is entirely due to the existing inequality in naval armaments, which is not suitable for Japan's national defense security and impairs its national prestige. Saito spoke with Hull for 15 minutes and concluded by saying that Japan does not intend to initiate the reopening of naval negotiations but is willing to cooperate with all countries to establish a new convention. If the United States, Britain, and Japan can agree on a common minimum naval limit, Japan is willing to abandon half of its existing navy. He does not fear that Japan's abrogation of the treaty may cause a naval race. All relevant people are very enlightened, and their governments are all rational. No one will engage in a damaging naval shipbuilding race. (Reuters, 29th)

(Washington) After conveying the official explanation of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Secretary of State Hull today, Ambassador Saito made his personal statement, expressing his confidence that the friendship between Japan and the United States in the past and the talents of statesmen will continue to maintain peace and establish a mutually satisfactory agreement. Saito also called for the establishment of a new treaty to achieve universal disarmament, saying that Japan has proposed the complete abolition of battleships and aircraft carriers and is prepared to reduce half of its existing naval strength. "We are willing to reduce as much as possible on both material and moral grounds to relieve all countries of the fear of war. We want other countries to have no fear of us, and we also want us to have no fear of other countries." Saito said that Japan's demand for equality is a prerequisite for reducing naval strength. "The major naval powers each have difficult tasks within their own countries and their respective spheres of influence. They have no time to consider fighting with other countries. Therefore, an agreement between the three countries should be established on a reasonable basis as soon as possible. Fortunately, there is still plenty of time to hesitate before the notification of abrogation takes effect, and even if a concrete agreement cannot be reached, I have no fear, because the people of the three countries are all knowledgeable, and the governments of the three countries are also deeply aware of the situation. No one wants to engage in a naval construction competition." Ambassador Saito expressed great satisfaction with the efforts of Japan and the United States to curb war rhetoric. His conclusion was, "I observe that the past friendship and the talents of statesmen in both countries have been able to solve many problems, so my hope always exists." (National News Agency, 29th)

Hull's Reply: Willing to Cooperate to Seek Peace; Equal Rights Must Consider National Defense Needs; US Always Relies on This as the Foundation of Diplomacy 24

(Washington) Hull's response takes a sympathetic attitude toward Japan, but expresses regret for Japan's actions. He said that all countries are now willing to treat other countries on a basis of absolute equality, but experience tells us that countries seek equality of armaments regardless of their different defense needs. This is not the way to promote peace or implement disarmament. Washington views Japan's treaty abrogation with regret, but we acknowledge that all countries have the right to reject the continuation of treaties. Any action tending towards disarmament must have voluntary consent in order to be effective. Seeking peace through disarmament and cooperation remains the basis of American foreign policy. The United States is willing to negotiate with all countries when there is hope of obtaining a mutually satisfactory outcome in order to prevent countries from being burdened by avoidable excessive military expenditure. (Reuters, 29th)

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull, after receiving the notification from Japan declaring the abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty, immediately sent a reply to Ambassador Saito stating that the notification had been received. He then issued a statement to the press stating that Japan had the right to declare the abrogation of the treaty, but this move was regrettable. Hull then referred to the London naval talks and their friendly and sincere spirit, saying that any country has the right to demand equality in security and peace, but merely demanding equality of armaments without considering the national defense needs of each country is of no benefit to disarmament. The Washington Naval Treaty stipulates methods for naval powers to cooperate in disarmament, making the peaceful environment even more fulfilling. Although Japan has declared the abrogation of the treaty, there are still two years until the expiration of the treaty, which allows time to consider the consequences of the complete abandonment of the treaty. Therefore, the United States is prepared to participate in future naval talks that can avoid the heavy burden of naval expenditure and satisfy the United States and other nations. Hull concluded, "The American nation, based on sincere friendship and the spirit of treating other nations, will continue to work hard to encourage other countries to emulate." (Havas, 29th)

US Transmits Copy of Japanese Notification to Britain, France, and Italy 25

(Washington) Japan's formal notification of the abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty was delivered by Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito to Secretary of State Hull a few minutes after noon today. The procedure took place in Hull's office. Coincidentally, outside the window was the memorial to the war dead of the European War. After Ambassador Saito arrived at the State Department, he quickly took the elevator to the office of the Secretary of State. Hull's doorman, the black man Daniel,

Page 8

entered the room to report. Hull immediately invited Saito inside, shook hands to show welcome, and closed the door for a private conversation. However, after receiving the Japanese notification, Hull immediately summoned his secretary to send copies of the notification to the representatives of the three signatory countries, Britain, France, and Italy. It is expected that they can be delivered today. According to government statements, the United States will formally notify Japan that it has received the notification. Although Washington is not surprised by the abrogation of the treaty, all government authorities deeply feel that Japan's actions are a retrogressive act against world peace. Some senior officials of the Navy Department blame the abrogation of the treaty on the United States because the United States did not expand its naval strength to the extent permitted by the treaty. They believe that the original 5:5:3 ratio was based on the original tonnage of the three countries, Britain, the United States, and Japan, but did not take into account the warships that were already being built in each country at that time. (National News Agency, 29th)

Britain Believes that Naval Compromise is Not Hopeless; Proposes to Reconcile American and Japanese Differences through Qualitative Disarmament 26

(London) The world's political circles today all regarded Japan's formal abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty as their sole topic of conversation. Britain and the United States are very disappointed that Japan has abandoned the treaty, which has been effective in limiting the expansion of armaments and reversing the naval race, but do not consider it hopeless. The hope that exists in the eyes of the British is that Japan has not revealed any intention to abolish the Nine-Power Treaty and the Four-Power Treaty. These two treaties, like the Washington Naval Treaty, are the organization of peace in the Pacific group. However, once the Washington Treaty is abolished, it will be possible to raise political questions when future naval talks are resumed. (Reuters, 30th)

(London) Japan has formally announced the abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty. This was expected. The impression from well-informed sources in Britain is that the declaration of abrogation is merely the end of one chapter in the naval issue. However, the system established by the Washington Naval Treaty has not collapsed. Therefore, the general concept is neither optimistic nor pessimistic. Official speeches by British figures often state that not only is it possible to reduce naval armaments, but it is also possible to reduce land and air force armaments. This is a phrase commonly used by officials. Recently, Foreign Secretary Simon declared in Parliament that equality in the quantity of armaments and seeking equality in security are two different issues. At the last few meetings between the British and American representatives, the British delegation declared to the American delegation that Britain had saved hundreds of millions of dollars in its budget and avoided serious incidents in diplomacy in the thirteen years since the Washington Naval Treaty was implemented. Therefore, Britain's desire to maintain the fundamental principles of the Washington Naval Treaty is the same as that of the United States. Now that the Washington Naval Treaty has been declared abolished by Japan, Britain does not believe that the naval disarmament issue has reached a point of no return. Because in the initial talks of this naval conference, both sides often used domestic public opinion as an excuse and insisted on not making concessions on principles that were difficult to disagree with. In fact, what both sides were arguing about was purely national dignity. Britain is fully aware of this. Moreover, since the dispute over naval issues, British figures, in light of the thinking of Japan and the United States, believe that if negotiations are conducted through diplomatic procedures, it may be easier to reconcile. Today, someone has said that Britain has a proposal prepared to seek a basis for compromise between the three countries on qualitative disarmament. Success in this matter will naturally take quite some time, but the fact that there is such a motivation on the day the treaty abrogation is announced shows that Britain's desire to achieve a compromise is very strong. With this desire, Britain will use all methods and do its best to mediate so that the next naval conference can be convened and achieve success. (Havas, 29th)

France Dissatisfied with the Treaty Due to Changing Circumstances; Naval Veteran Publishes an Article Advocating that All Countries Continue to Conclude New Agreements; Air Forces Should Also be Subject to Limitations 27

(Paris) The Morning Post published an article by Admiral de Taokudier today, stating that when the Washington Naval Treaty was signed in 1922 and the London Naval Treaty was signed in 1930, the German Navy had not been reorganized and the Italian Navy was insignificant. Now that times have changed, France sincerely approves of the declaration of abrogation of the two treaties by legal procedures. If this were not the case, our position would be even more inferior within three years. Therefore, the best plan for now is to immediately conclude a new agreement that is more fair and based on the current situation, which is different from the situation in 1922. However, will Germany and Soviet Russia participate in a new naval conference to negotiate a new naval agreement in the future? Moreover, due to the rapid advancement of aviation technology, there is a great possibility for the development of naval air force armaments. Then, can this new naval agreement, which does not include limitations on air force armaments, be concluded separately? Or even further, there are many dependencies in the Pacific, and all colonial countries are related to the naval and air force bases there. Therefore, the issue of naval and air force bases in the Pacific should be re-examined. (Havas, 30th)

Italy's View: Japanese Action Violates Italian Policy and Risks Promoting an Arms Race 28

(Rome) Italy understands Japan's view of treaty abrogation, but feels that this action violates Italy's disarmament policy and contains the danger of promoting an arms race. The treaty is particularly important to Italy because it stipulates that France allows Italy to be equal to it in capital ships. (Reuters, 29th)

The Americans hope that the powers can meet again next year, but all matters will depend on Japan's attitude.

Italy Proposes a Compromise Plan with the Focus on Maintaining Austrian Independence as a Guarantee for Central European Peace; Italy Takes the Lead, and France is Expected to Draft a Compromise Plan 31

(Paris) Regarding the Italian proposal to guarantee peace in Central Europe, a Paris newspaper reported today that France has drafted a compromise plan. The main idea is to divide the Central European political organization into two major parts. It is said that Italy's plan to guarantee Austrian independence will be jointly supported by Italy, Germany, Hungary, Czechoslovakia, and Yugoslavia. However, if Germany and Hungary are unwilling to sign, their positions can be left vacant, and the agreement's effectiveness will still come into effect immediately. After the first step of this diplomatic procedure is implemented, it will be followed by a second step, establishing a Central European guarantee agreement broadly based on the Balkan Entente. This agreement should also be signed by France and Romania. In this way, Italy and the Little Entente countries will be able to mutually guarantee their borders, as safeguarding borders is the fundamental goal of French foreign policy. Indian Governor-General Warns Gandhi Not to Engage in Non-Violent Resistance Again; Otherwise, Stern Measures Will Be Taken 34

Previously, Gandhi, on behalf of the All-India National Congress, announced the end of the civil disobedience movement, but reserved the right to personally engage in disobedience to achieve Indian autonomy. Recently, Gandhi wanted to go to the Frontier Province to promote rural economic revitalization, but the Governor-General rejected this. The Governor-General, fearing that Gandhi might resume the disobedience movement and need to be arrested, sought instructions from London. The British government seemed to advocate punishment as well. However, because Gandhi's physical condition is weak, they feared he might not be able to withstand the stimulation, and if anything unexpected happened, it would cause an accident. Therefore, they advocated only giving a warning. However, Gandhi believes that "disobedience" is a "right endowed to mankind since birth" and has always insisted on it. Therefore, the Governor-General of India will likely take stern measures. (29th Havas)

Perpetrators of Kirov Assassination Case: Fourteen Terrorist Group Members Sentenced to Death for Conspiring to Overthrow the Government with Foreign Assistance; Zinoviev and Kamenev to be Tried by Special Tribunal 37

(Moscow) Nikolai Nikolaev, the murderer of Kirov, and thirteen other Communist Party members involved in the case were sentenced to death today by the Supreme Military Tribunal. The sentences were carried out by firing squad immediately after the verdict was announced. All the convicts' property was confiscated by the government. According to an official announcement on the trial proceedings, former members of Zinoviev's group, which opposed the Soviet government, had organized a counter-revolutionary terrorist organization in Leningrad. The defendants were members of this organization. The organization's purpose was to disrupt the Soviet Russian government through terrorist actions and to change the current policy to "Zinoviev and Trotsky's" policy. The organization also wanted to provoke foreign military intervention. Therefore, the murderer Nikolai Nikolaev met with a consul of a certain country in Leningrad in order to achieve this goal. The defendants, acting on the orders of their headquarters in Leningrad, conspired and assassinated Kirov on the first of this month. As for Zinoviev and Kamenev, they will be tried by a special tribunal in a few days. Both of these men were assistants to Lenin in creating the Soviet Russian government. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

Compatriots Expelled from Japan Return to Qingdao 72

Li Jingxing Describes Oppression

Qingdao Correspondence: Regarding the Japanese expulsion of overseas Chinese, our government has repeatedly protested, but with no satisfactory results. Now, another 22 overseas Chinese compatriots, including Huang Enrong, Li Jingxing, and Lin Wanqing, have been expelled and returned to their country. On the 26th of this month, they arrived in Qingdao from Moji, Japan, aboard the Nikko Maru. After disembarking, Huang and the others went to the police station of the 3rd branch of the dock public security bureau to report their experiences of being expelled from Japan. Huang and Lin went to the Zhongxing Button Factory in Taitong Town to stay, while Li Jingxing stayed at the Taihe Inn on Taian Road. The rest were scattered in various inns. According to Li Jingxing, "I am from Zouping and was engaged in the sale of jade and coral in Japan. Huang Enrong and Lin Wanqing are from Zhaoyuan and ran a restaurant at the Yokohama dock. Most overseas Chinese in Japan live in Osaka and Tokyo, followed by Yokohama and Kobe. Most overseas Chinese from North China are engaged in commerce, while those from South China mostly run restaurants or sell their labor. However, the Japanese have recently been very discriminatory towards overseas Chinese, using all means of humiliation and exploitation, and simply do not treat them as human beings. This is all because of our weakness. When the Japanese see us, they often say, 'All the Japanese money has been earned by you.' Now, the Japanese can still tolerate wealthy overseas Chinese, but for those without money, such as laborers and us merchants, they mostly find small faults without reason, detain them in Japanese government offices, and forcibly send them back to their home country when there is a ship available, unwilling to tolerate them for a moment. Those working in Japan used to earn more than two yuan a day, but now it has been reduced to one yuan or eight jiao, and most are unable to make a living. However, the Japanese are still afraid that the overseas Chinese will take their jobs, so they deposit all the surplus of the overseas Chinese's daily wages, except for room and board, on their behalf, and when there is enough money for the return trip, they are expelled back to their country, unwilling to tolerate them for a moment. In recent years, I don't know how many batches of overseas Chinese have been expelled back to their country by the Japanese. I remember that last time there were 26 overseas Chinese who were expelled back to their country, five of whom had married Japanese women. The feelings between the couples were very good, and the Japanese women also wanted to come to China with their husbands. Who knew that when they arrived in Kobe, they were forcibly detained by the Japanese police. The reason for my (Li referring to himself) expulsion this time was that on the 13th and 14th of this month, I joked with a waitress (female) in a Japanese restaurant, and the Japanese suspected that I had committed adultery. They immediately reported it to the police, and without asking questions, they forcibly sent me back to my country. In short, it is very dangerous for overseas Chinese in Japan who are laborers and merchants. Now, they are returning in batches, which has a great impact on people's livelihoods. But what can our weak China do to help? This time, there were six of us who were sent to the ship together in Yokohama, and the rest were sent on in Moji. When we left, the Japanese police led us to the Chinese consulate and said that they wanted to send us back to our country. The consulate had no way to help and could only let them do as they pleased. Now that we have returned to our country, I would rather starve to death in my own country than go back to Japan to be bullied by them." He was overcome with sadness. (26th)

Page 9

The Fate of the Okada Cabinet (Japanese Dispatch) Party Decline, Okada Ascends, Limited Finances, Takahashi Returns 73

When Keisuke Okada, a naval admiral, first formed his cabinet, it was derided as second-rate. This was because he himself was not a politician, and he lacked a clear political program capable of rallying the masses. He was merely being used by elder statesmen and influential figures as a symbol of constitutional government, to ease the conflict between civilian and military rule, in the expectation that an opportunity would arise in the future to restore constitutional government. Another very important matter was the so-called crisis of 1936, which was particularly acute in the maritime sphere. It was truly not easy for Japan to find a suitable figure capable of harmonizing military affairs, politics, finance, and the economy.

The previous Prime Minister, Makoto Saito, seemed broad-minded and tolerant, allowing the ministers in his cabinet to manage their respective departments independently. In particular, both the army and navy were able to fully exert their abilities. Unexpectedly, the "Teikoku Rayon Company" bribery case implicated Finance Vice-Minister Kuroda through the Bank of Taiwan. At the same time, Finance Minister Takahashi also bore responsibility for negligence or inadequate supervision of his subordinates. As a result, the Saito cabinet was naturally embarrassed to continue. However, its mission – to overcome the extraordinary period – had not yet ended. Therefore, after consultation among elder statesmen and influential figures, Okada was recommended to take office, with the aim of extending the Saito cabinet. The underlying intention was to prevent the hardliners in the military (who advocated national socialism) from overstepping their bounds, and to find a way to overcome the difficult hurdle of the naval disarmament conference. Okada himself had considerable experience in military and political affairs, but he was not very adept in politics. However, he was a very simple and honest man, and he was well-regarded within the navy. Therefore, his appointment as Prime Minister at this time had a moderating effect. However, his debating skills were very poor, and his ability to handle the Diet was truly lacking. In the past, during the extraordinary session of the Diet, Seiwa-kai Diet member Ando Junsei questioned Vice-Minister Tanaka of the Colonial Affairs Ministry about his reasons for resigning. Okada's answer was that Tanaka had been recommended by the Minseito party, and that the matter should be addressed to the Minseito party. His response was inadequate, and he later realized he had misspoken and retracted his answer. Such incidents occurred several times during the extraordinary session. If the Diet had authority and could uphold the spirit of parliamentary politics, then the Prime Minister's irresponsible and incoherent responses would have at least caused an uproar. The reason why he was able to pass through unscathed was that the Diet had fundamentally lost its ability to control politics, and the shortcomings of the political parties were all too obvious, so they had no choice but to let the government do as it pleased.

Another aspect of the Okada cabinet that grasped the demands of the times was the reinstatement of Takahashi Korekiyo as Finance Minister. Originally, Fujii Shinobu had been in disagreement with the military over budget issues, and the revenue was insufficient. If taxes were increased according to the military's demands, it would further provoke the dissatisfaction of capitalists and the criticism of the media. Fujii resigned on the eve of the opening of the extraordinary session of the Diet. If a suitable person could not be found, the Okada cabinet might have collapsed.

Takahashi Korekiyo had served as president of the Seiyukai party and was a veteran of Japanese politics. His wife was from Satsuma, and his sister was married to the younger brother of Makino Nobuaki. Through blood ties, he had deep connections with the Satsuma clique (the naval clique). Takahashi himself had previously served as Finance Minister six times and was very familiar with Japan's dire political situation and economic conditions. Moreover, he had a particularly good rapport with both the army and navy. After the fall of the Terauchi cabinet in 1918, Army Minister Tanaka Giichi and Navy Minister Kato Tomosaburo competed to expand their armaments. When the Hara cabinet was almost unable to resolve the situation, Takahashi stepped in to mediate. He believed that while their "emphasis on national defense was certainly correct, it was even more important to pay attention to national strength – if financial strength was not taken into consideration, then national defense was equivalent to a pie painted on paper..." Therefore, both the army and navy believed that he was acting in the interests of the country and respected him accordingly. Even now, it remains the same. When Araki Sadao was Army Minister, he was truly independent and dismissive of everyone, but he was still very impressed by Takahashi. Therefore, he released 10 million yen from the army's budget to the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, saving the previous cabinet from a crisis.

This time, Takahashi's reinstatement as Finance Minister was well-received by financial capital because of his superior economic expertise and his exceptional familiarity with the state of the Japanese national economy. The military also highly respected him, making him the foremost figure in the current cabinet. The Okada cabinet was thus temporarily stabilized. The 67th session of the Diet, which opened today, could do nothing about the government, or else it would have to be dissolved. (Tokyo, December 24, 1934)

Chairman Chiang's Visit to Hangzhou 74

Grand Welcome Rally Held This Morning at the New Games

Hangzhou Dispatch: Military Affairs Commission Chairman Chiang, having completed his ancestral grave sweeping in his hometown and with his toothache gradually subsiding, arrived in Hangzhou yesterday (29th) morning at 9:00 a.m., accompanied by his wife, Madame Soong Mei-ling, Central Supervisory Committee member Wang Chonghui, Song Zi'an of the Songjiang Salt Transport Office, and others, traveling by automobile from Fenghua via the Fengxin-Shao-Cao-Sheng highway. Northwestern Fujian Remnant Bandits Suffered a Crushing Defeat

Fuzhou Dispatch: After Chiang Ting-wen assumed the position of Pacification Commissioner of Fujian, he scheduled a province-wide pacification conference for early January of the 24th year of the Republic, to be held in Zhangzhou, convening the commanders and deputy commanders of the eastern, western, southern, and northern districts of Fujian, as well as the division commanders stationed in the province. Therefore, he is currently only convening the commanders of the northeastern districts to give them instructions in person. A plan has been formulated. Chiang has now completed his official business and is scheduled to leave the province and return to Zhangzhou in four or five days.

After all counties in northwestern Fujian were completely recovered, the remaining bandits numbered only a little over two thousand, entrenched in the Quanshang Wucun area in the jurisdiction of Ninghua County, at the center of the border between Mingxi, Qingliu, Jianning, and Jiangle counties.
