Economic Supplement

Reflections on Holding a National Goods Year 240

— Liu Tang

Purchasing and using national goods is the natural duty of citizens, and striving to produce national products to meet needs is also the basic responsibility of citizens. There is no need for promotion or supervision. However, the situation in our country is very different. Clothes are not beautiful unless they are "foreign," food is insufficient unless it is "foreign," housing is incomplete unless it is "foreign," and travel is not fast unless it is "foreign." Daily necessities and the resources for food and clothing all rely on "foreign" goods. The domestically produced goods, whether natural or artificial, are almost unmatched. As a result, farmland is desolate, looms are idle, and handicrafts are bankrupt. Even the so-called "national goods," which are actually "machine-made imitations of foreign goods," are like candles flickering in the wind, uncertain. At this time, people recognize the endless economic invasion from abroad and the lack of control, and strive to promote the national goods movement.

However, what is the result of promoting national goods? It cannot be said that there is no effect, but after twenty years of effort, the so-called "national goods" still seem to be in their infancy, unable to keep pace with the times, which is very sad. Looking back at the year after the January 28th Incident (1933), deeply aware of the increasing foreign troubles, the backwardness of industry, and the pressure of the economic tide, the call for a "National Goods Year" was made. In that year, the citizens had not forgotten the pain of artillery and airplanes, so they received widespread support. The most obvious change was that men's coarse cloth gowns and women's checkered cloth robes became popular for a while, and the coarse cloth stores had a turnaround in business. By this year (1935), it was designated as "Women's National Goods Year." Women are the backbone of household purchases. Department stores often rely on whether they can get women's patronage and trust to predict the prosperity or decline of their business. This trend is particularly obvious overseas. If Shanghai women gradually become fond of shopping in stores and are happy to purchase national goods, then the promotion of national goods will be like water flowing downwards, reaching everywhere. Who would have thought that a year would pass quickly? Although the elimination of millions of dollars in perfumes and creams, the disappearance of checkered cloth robes, and the decline of coarse cloth business cannot be taken as signs of the failure of Women's National Goods Year, the extravagance and luxury of Shanghai women, competing for novelty and beauty, have not changed from the past.

The promotion of "National Goods Year" is a kind of stimulant, like giving a heart medicine to a weak heart, seeking temporary maintenance, and then seeking fundamental treatment. If it continues, it will eventually be ineffective, because stimulants only have stimulating effects and have no fundamental therapeutic power. The same is true for publicity. Although it is called publicity, there must be facts to prove it in the end. If you only do publicity, after a long time, even if the speakers are earnest, the listeners will be dismissive. For example, the annual ×× National Goods Year, the people in charge have good intentions, because only in this way can they receive great results, so they use the method of dividing years and planning stages. If it is women, if it is students, ... expanding and enriching it, then it may as well be parents, workers, farmers, ... gradually promoting it to all walks of life. Then national goods will spread without legs. Only do not think that society is a whole society, and family is a whole family. Holding them separately, those who do not know will misunderstand that this Women's National Goods Year has nothing to do with men; this Student National Goods Year has nothing to do with parents; perhaps there is no such fact, but it cannot prevent people from thinking this way. If propaganda makes people think one more time, or make one more exception, then its effectiveness will be reduced to some extent. Therefore, even with hundreds of theories, it is not as good as one point of fact. King Yue of Yue's ten years of living and ten years of teaching eventually defeated Wu; Duke Wen of Wei's coarse cloth clothes and large silk hats eventually revived because of his ability to act. Today, when talking about national goods, even children know the necessity of it. If you ask about the facts, then you will know that it is not so. Drawing paper, painting colors, as well as suits and leather shoes, household items, ... if children ask teachers and parents, what words will the teachers and parents use to answer, or will they speak separately, this is a cultural product, this is a necessity, use it out of necessity, or will they simply avoid arguing it! If they cannot, then they have already used foreign goods, and they persuade others to use national goods. How will this kind of self-deceiving and deceiving impression, left in the minds of pure children, affect them? If you want to establish yourself, establish others. If you want to correct yourself, correct others. What you do not want, do not impose on others. How can you personally commit it?

However, I am not saying that the national goods propaganda movement is unnecessary. Being able to promote is better than not promoting, and being able to publicize is better than not publicizing. Only after twenty years of promoting and publicizing, we still have not achieved great results. In the end, I feel that in addition to publicity and promotion, there should be other efforts. The problem still lies in only knowing how to persuade people to use national goods, but not being able to supply people with national goods, and not being able to make people happy to use national goods without complaining. Therefore, in the future, we should think more from the perspective of facts, and put less effort into theory. We should think more from the perspective of production, and do less publicity from the perspective of consumption. We should shift the spirit of National Goods Year, which focuses on consumption, to the work of working together to promote production in order to achieve self-sufficiency through use. Because there is good production, there will be good sales. If there is no good production, and people are persuaded to use it necessarily, even countries with deep-rooted economic aggression like ours can easily induce the import of foreign goods. Readers should not misunderstand that I am defending foreign goods, because the facts are like this. No matter who chooses to buy goods, they must use "cheap and good" as the standard. Even national goods manufacturers purchase materials, why not do the same? Purchasing less durable goods at a higher price is already what buyers are unwilling to do, let alone... Although purchasing national goods, sometimes it is not allowed to calculate every penny, and the overall benefit should be taken into account, national goods manufacturers should also consider the interests of the public users. If they sell non-durable goods to people, manufacturers can use the name of patriotism to sell goods and seek wealth, but if they make people turn to foreign goods because national goods are not durable or the prices are not appropriate, wouldn't it be the same as bearing the responsibility of promoting the sales of foreign goods? We have boycotted Japanese goods again and again, but every time we boycott, the import volume of Japanese goods will increase once. This is not only true in China, but in Europe, America, Southeast Asia and other places, Japanese goods can also be continuously invaded. In the interview record of Japanese Minister of Finance Takahashi Korekiyo published in the Current Affairs News (23, 12, 18), one can think about more than half of it. He said:

"Although countries boycott Japanese goods, Japanese goods are still exported continuously, and the voice of boycott has gradually subsided recently, because my Japanese (Takahashi claims) commodities are cheap and good, ranking first in the world. Would people in various countries rather buy inferior goods at a high price? For example, in Sino-Japanese trade, according to the latest news from the Commercial Affairs Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, our country's (Japan's) exports are increasing day by day, especially rayon. Although there are some anti-Japanese people in your country (China) who are making trouble from it (?), it is still able to sell without hindrance because of the low price..."

It is not surprising that these words come from a high-ranking official, but Chinese people - especially national goods manufacturers - cannot but feel deeply ashamed. Why do we boycott, but it is just empty talk, without any practical effect? And why can't our country's products be "cheap and good" and make people happy to use them? "On the contrary, seek it from yourself", is it because you focus too much on publicity, seek too little for reality, embellish the scene, and waste your reputation? Therefore, there is no other way but for the masses to do their best, seek truth from facts, and bury their heads in hard work.

Actual work, to put it in a small way, is like the formal attire movement of the Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Association, which is also a good method; to put it in a long way, is like the rumor that officials in Beijing Municipal Government with a salary of more than sixty yuan should purchase a satin gown, and the notice from the Lake Society that all members will wear blue robes and black jackets for the New Year's Day group worship. Although the matter is small, its effect is huge. Someone said, in a broad sense, why not say silk fabrics. But today, silk fabrics are neither welcomed by modern women nor rejected by eyebrow men. I once said that if women wear a few less pairs of high-heeled leather shoes, and men make a few less suits, if they can completely change to silk fabrics, the benefits to the silk cocoon and silk satin industry are already not insignificant. As for the formal attire movement, in a world confused by woolen foreign goods, it is already clearly defined by government laws and regulations. If this cannot be implemented, what else is enough! How can you say that you are promoting national goods?

To put it in a larger way:

(2) How to Make People Happy to Use National Goods

This requires the efforts of national goods manufacturers themselves, which is the word "cheap and good" that is difficult to say but difficult to do. The so-called cheap and good is originally a comparative term. You want the price to be cheap and the quality to be good, a bear's paw is what I want, and fish is what I want, there are very few things in the world that can have both; but at least, always make people feel that buying this thing is "worth it", and the word "worth it" is the foundation of happiness. We don't need to use medicine as an analogy, but we hear that foreign goods are made of the same materials and labor. The labor in foreign countries is more expensive than in China, and they have to travel across the ocean to transport them to China, plus water fees, freight, taxes, insurance, etc. Why can they still sell without hindrance? Why is the goods of this factory suppressed by it? Of course, the "worship of foreign" psychology of the Chinese people is too despicable, which leads to this, and the goods of this factory cannot seek progress in technology, lose the trust of customers, and help the promotion of foreign goods. It seems that they cannot escape the blame.

Furthermore, the biggest drawback of national goods is that if a kind of goods can be sold, either the price will be high, or a hundred kinds of inferior goods will be produced, or imitations will arise, so that it is difficult to distinguish between good and bad, and it is difficult to distinguish between the good and the bad. There are already many people who mix fish eyes with pearls, and the buyers turn their heads and all die together. Therefore, manufacturers do not seek people's trust from commercial ethics, and do not seek people to use from the improvement of products, but want to use the power of propaganda, the power of words, the name of patriotism, and the help of laws to make people use them. This is contrary to the development of national goods, and it will be ineffective if it is implemented for a hundred years; only good production can have good sales; with good sales, foreign goods will naturally be cut off, and national goods will naturally prosper. Therefore, I hope that national goods manufacturers:

(A) Standardize products

(B) Refine finished products

(C) Sell goods at reasonable prices

(D) Industry cooperation

These four are the keys to success. All are not in propaganda, but in hard work.

(2) How to Meet People's Needs

This refers to quantity. Today, national goods manufacturers have how many percent of foreign goods? Before the analysis, it is difficult to get an overview, but it can be guaranteed that there are very few. There are only a handful of heavy industries, and only a small number of applied industries. It is very difficult to compete with foreign goods. In terms of quantity, it is even less worth mentioning. If you want people to buy them like this, and people really buy them, how will you respond? In the end, it is either shoddy manufacturing, or changing the head and face, using other people's products to act as their own. If this is the case, it is no different from promoting counterfeit national goods, which is completely contrary to the purpose of promotion. Therefore, if you want to promote a certain product, you must first check the content and production volume of the product. If you know that it is not enough to apply, or you don't know what its content is, and you think it can be applied, it is like a child learning to walk, forcing him to walk. If he does not stumble, he must be supported by someone. Therefore, manufacturers also want the product to be used by people, and should also think about how many consumers can be satisfied by the product. If it can replace foreign goods, everyone is happy to buy it, and the strength is enough to meet this demand. If not, what method will be used to supplement it? We should also start from the foreign goods and domestic products. If we can divide the work and plan the steps to gradually realize it, it is the most important thing at present.

(3) How to Adapt to People's Needs

Hobbies are different, and needs are different. Therefore, how to adapt to people's needs is what national goods manufacturers should know and should also respond to. The reason why foreigners' trade is always successful is that they pay attention to the likes and dislikes of customs and the changes in hobbies, so they can cater to people's preferences and satisfy people's desires. The same is true for their own plans. For example, the British love tea, so they transplanted tea trees to Ceylon. Italy and France like silk weaving, so they raise silkworms and mulberry trees. Americans need tung oil, so they collect tung seeds. The Japanese saw that silkworm silk was expensive and high-priced, and worried that it would be defeated by rayon, so they rushed to make rayon, and they have been able to have a large number of exports in addition to self-sufficiency, competing with European and American production in the market. The same is true for other handicrafts. What about our country? Foreigners are still trying to adapt to our needs, but we cannot respond ourselves. Superiority wins and inferiority fails, and the situation is clear. Therefore, in general, we think there is a need, and we should find a way to adapt to it. Whether this can be successful depends on the cooperation of all parties, but national goods manufacturers are the core of it. How can they not cheer up and do it?

(4) How to Inspire People's Needs

Adapting to people's needs seems to be insufficient, and we should go further and inspire people's needs. The so-called inspiration of people's needs is also like the saying "look and buy", "look" originally has no intention of "buy", "if you see it well, you might as well buy it"; on the one hand, it is because they have the purchasing power, and on the other hand, it is because this item is enough to touch their desire and arouse their need. If everything is only adapted to the present, it will not be able to progress and will lead to failure. Therefore, it can create and develop; there is production and consumption; this evolution is also the key to the evolution of human groups. Shanghai stores have also recently posted "welcome to visit" signs. Although it is said so, when you step into the door, you often leave with an unpleasant impression. Why? It lies in the improper handling, which turns into a burden for its business.

As for why domestic industry and commerce have failed; in terms of themselves, we can also get the following points:

(1) Lack of Business Talents

In the fiercely competitive industrial and commercial enterprises, it is difficult to cope with the old organization and talents. Those who do not know their own limits do not think it is insufficient, but those who know it have never failed to worry deeply. The vision, understanding, spirit, and actions of the current operators of industrial and commercial enterprises should be able to adapt to the modern trend in all aspects. However, in our country, most people do not know what organization is, what the general trend is, and they are short-sighted and have little knowledge. Therefore, they can only be in good times, and they can only get small profits. Once they encounter adversity, they will be at a loss. They cannot stabilize themselves, and others can do nothing to help. Therefore, when the difficult times come, there is no way to save them. Even worse, they may affect others and suffer the disaster of the pond fish. There are countless cases.

I have heard that many industrial and commercial enterprises are difficult to improve because of the poor organization in the past; the habits are too deep and difficult to correct; the machinery is outdated and the products are difficult to refine; even if there are talents, they cannot do anything. It is difficult to hope for progress without major reforms. If you want to reform urgently, obstacles will arise and difficulties will gather. The best example is the ×× Printing House. After the reorganization after a major accident, everything is different from the past, but the managers are not the same people before and after; the reason why it can be like this is that the old bad state has disappeared with the artillery fire, and it is not difficult to completely transform it from scratch to meet the needs of the times, and there is today's result. There are many Chinese industrial and commercial enterprises similar to this, what else can I say!

(2) Lack of Management Talents

The ability of the factory to produce fine and cheap products is closely related to the management talents; if the management is not good, the materials will be wasted, the working hours will not be economical, the products will not be refined, the costs will increase, and the sales will be difficult. The current factory management personnel often cannot have both, that is, (1) have experience but no knowledge, (2) have knowledge but no experience. Those who have experience but no knowledge are mostly foremen who came from workers; those who have knowledge but no experience are students who came from schools; those who have experience but no knowledge do not know how to improve and stick to the old methods; those who have knowledge but no experience only talk about theories and lack practicality; each should have a way to remedy it. The former should set up remedial classes to teach new knowledge, so that they can improve; the latter must first have sufficient practice in the engineering they manage before they can be actually authorized at the beginning of their employment; I heard that Japan also had this problem at first, and after this correction, it has today's achievements.

(3) Lack of Technical Talents

Technical talents are the mentors of factory products. It is the responsibility of technical talents to promote the old and produce new, and to make products refined. Although the Chinese people say that they have changed their old ideas, secretly observing the general public, the old thoughts and habits have not been completely transformed. Therefore, the cultivation of technical talents is not as many as the text and economic ones; even if there are some technical talents, they are often "heroes have no place to use their talents", and they abandon what they have learned. Talents are needed in other aspects, but there is nowhere to seek them. Half of the talents are buried because they cannot be adjusted, and half are lost in training. People often say that science can save the country. In the future, we should have the spirit of respecting scientists and cultivate technical talents to solve the current difficulties of industry and commerce.

(4) Lack of Workers' Skills

The success of factory products, although under the guidance of technicians and managers, is made by the hands of workers; therefore, the quality of workers' skills is closely related to the quality of products. Because of the lack of education, workers in our country often do not know a word, and even in their work, they only know what it is, but do not know why it is, so it is difficult to have progress. Furthermore, workers have recently been seeking to improve and increase their living standards and treatment from time to time; but they have not seen their efforts to improve the efficiency of their work; even the work has regressed, and the efficiency has decreased, resulting in increased costs and degraded products. Therefore, how to improve the discipline, service, and skills of workers is of great importance to Chinese industry and commerce.

In addition, such as lack of capital, and lack of flexibility in turnover, it is not easy to develop. In particular, the desire to seek immediate benefits is too urgent, so there is no long-term plan, it is difficult to fight a protracted war, and it is easy to be controlled by others. Some people think that the financial industry does not invest in industrial and commercial preparation, I am not a member of the financial industry, and I have nothing to do with the left and right wings, but the only condition for the investment of the financial industry is safety, that is, the possibility of recovering its principal and interest. Today, whether the industry and commerce themselves are sound, I dare not make a general statement, but if the organization is precise, and it is indeed in financial difficulties but has a promising future, if the financial industry does not help it, then its intention is questionable.

In addition to the internal defects, Chinese industry and commerce also have external infringements. Here, I will focus on the aspects that are closely related to national goods factories to save space:

(1) Material Issues

The so-called national goods now, to be honest, can be said to be processed and manufactured products of foreign goods, because the materials used are mostly foreign goods, so it is still difficult to compete with foreign goods for a day's growth. Foreign businessmen know that a certain material is a competitor to their certain goods, then they may as well raise the price when ordering materials, so that their products are still difficult to compete with foreign goods, this is one. Furthermore, those who can protect industry and commerce and resist foreign countries use tariff barriers to block them, but for countries that cannot supply their own materials, such as raising tariffs, it is no different from increasing the cost of domestic products. Thirdly, if all materials and supplies are supplied by imports, it is no different from handing the power of life and death of our industry to foreign merchants, and we will never be able to get rid of their shackles, and there will be no day to eliminate them. Therefore, the whole country should work together to promote the success of the following matters:

(1) Material self-sufficiency, should be phased and divided into industries, and the implementation should be planned from all aspects, and the final goal of self-production and self-sufficiency should be achieved;

(2) For important industrial products, the materials of which cannot be obtained from abroad, the import tax should be reduced to a certain level;

(3) The import tax on unnecessary edible products (such as seafood, vegetable head food, etc.) and the same type of foreign goods whose products from domestic industry and commerce can勉可應付應 be increased to prevent dumping;

(4) We should do our best to improve agricultural products, build water conservancy, and develop mineral products in order to enrich materials;

The above concerns the self-sufficiency of materials and also involves tariff issues.

(2) Factory Establishment Issues

Since the Treaty of Shimonoseki between China and Japan caused a great mistake, allowing foreign merchants to also set up factories in trading ports and treat them equally with Chinese merchants, it was originally not surprising; but in a country where our industrial and commercial knowledge and skills are childish, what we can rely on to contend with foreign merchants is only the geographical convenience and cheap labor. Now that we share it with foreign merchants, our financial resources are inferior to others, our technology is inferior to others, and our management is inferior to others. How can we live with them in one place? The advantages and disadvantages of Sino-Japanese textile factories can already be seen in general. After the increase in tariffs, the psychology of foreign merchants to set up factories locally to manufacture is more firm, so the number of facts that have been expressed is unknown; if we allow it to continue to advance, the poison will be worse than the import of foreign goods, and Chinese merchants' factories will inevitably be a catastrophe and cannot be saved. The so-called "bone gangrene" is also. Talking about abolishing the treaty, I don't know how many treaties that have expired should be abolished but have not been abolished, so there is no need to talk about it. What I hope from the authorities is only to increase the factory tax and raise the bonus for Chinese merchants' factories. If there is only an increase in taxes without giving bonuses to Chinese merchants, then it will destroy its own industry and commerce, what else can I say!

Review of China's Coal Mining Industry in the 23rd Year of the Republic of China 241

— Zhu Wenqing

According to Mr. Weng Wenhao's estimate in 1932, China's coal reserves amounted to 240.81 million tons. Shanxi Province accounted for the largest share, totaling 127.127 million tons, exceeding 50% of the total reserves. The four northeastern provinces, which had been forcibly occupied by the Japanese, also had 4.61 million tons. Here, we must pay attention to one fact: the coal-bearing areas in China have not been fully developed; however, in areas such as the four northeastern provinces, which are under the control of foreign capital, the degree of development is quite high. The investment of foreign powers in Chinese coal mines is more than three times that of Chinese capital. Shanxi, the richest coal-bearing province, only produced 760,000 tons of coal in 1932, while the four northeastern provinces produced more than 8 million tons annually, Hebei produced more than 6 million tons, Henan produced 1.6 million tons, and Shandong produced more than 1.5 million tons. The coal industry in the four northeastern provinces has now become the source of military supply industries. The Fushun coal mine is the biggest threat to Chinese and even British investment in Chinese coal mines. Of the 6.6 to 7 million tons of coal produced in Hebei Province, more than 90% is produced by British capital; one mine alone produces around 6 million tons annually. Furthermore, some Chinese-owned coal companies have already mortgaged parts of their assets to Japan. Henan Province produces approximately 1.6 million tons of coal annually. Here, the British-owned Fu Company holds a dominant position. Although the Zhongyuan Company is currently sending personnel to reorganize and reduce workers, it has long been under the control of the Fu Company. The Liuhegou coal mine is also a famous coal-producing area in Henan Province and is currently managed by the Sino-Japanese Industrial Company, which, in other words, has already fallen into the hands of Japanese capital.

The Shandong Province seems to be the only one with a relatively strong presence of national capital. In 1932, Shandong's output was 1.57 million tons, of which 540,000 tons were produced by the Japanese-owned Luda Coal Mine, and the rest was produced by Chinese-owned enterprises. As for coal mines in other regions, such as the Pingxiang Coal Mine, which is entirely under Japanese control, there is no room for development. Although Shanxi's coal reserves are abundant, this only arouses the insatiable desire of foreign powers and does not help the development of national enterprises. Shanxi Province's controlled economy policy has not only failed to gradually develop the province's industries but has also led to "goods being abandoned on the ground" due to the heavy transportation costs and taxes, preventing development. The Tianjin Dagongbao published the following record on January 18, 1934: "The coal freight rate across the country is the highest on the Zhengtai Railway, and the freight rates set by the railway also vary greatly for each mine. ... A freight rate of 7 li per ton-mile for railway coal transport is the standard international rate. Although the BeiNing Railway for Beipiao coal, the XiangE Railway for Hanzhi coal, and the Jiaoji Railway for Luda Mine may not fully meet the 7 li rate, the difference is not significant. However, the Zhengtai Railway charges 0.024 yuan per ton per kilometer for Shanxi coal, which translates to 0.047 yuan per mile, which is five to six times higher than the international rate, and four to five times higher than the freight rates on other Chinese railways." Here, we must point out that the railways mentioned above, whose freight rates are not significantly different from the international rate, transport Beipiao coal, Luda coal, and Hanzhi coal, etc., all of which belong to foreign capital. In other words, foreign-owned coal can enjoy lower freight rates, while purely domestic coal cannot enjoy this preferential treatment. Thus, it can be seen that all Chinese railways discriminate against foreign and domestic goods.

The above is the general situation of China's coal mining industry. Now, we want to trace the general situation of the past year. Under the conditions of the deepening global economic panic and the increasing activity of foreign capital in China, China's national economy is heading towards a dead end of total bankruptcy. China's self-operated coal industry is naturally no exception. The consumption of coal is decreasing day by day due to the weakness of the general public's purchasing power and the shutdown and reduction of work in general factories. As a result, the price of coal is also falling rapidly. Let's take the coal produced by Kailuan as an example.

Price Fluctuation Table for Kailuan Coal (Unit: Yuan)

| | No. 2 Lump | No. 1 Powder | No. 2 Powder |

|--------|----------|----------|----------|

| 1933 | | | |

| December| 10.8 | 10.9 | 9.1 |

| 1934 | | | |

| January | 10.1 | 10.1 | 9.1 |

| June | 10.1 | 9.6 | 8.6 |

Although the nominal price of coal increased somewhat between October and December 1934, the actual price was below the low price in June. At the end of the year, coal merchants had to sell at reduced prices to obtain cash due to financial constraints, so the price of coal was even more likely to fall.

Now, we want to look at the amount of coal imported into Shanghai. We do not have accurate figures for the import volume in November and December, so we have to assume that the import volume in those two months is similar to the same period in 1933 (in reality, it is clearly decreasing). The figures should be as follows:

1931: 3,617,000 tons

1932: 2,942,276 tons

1933: 3,329,358 tons

1934: 3,192,767 tons

Compared with the previous year, 1934 decreased by about 140,000 tons. Here, we must also point out that the quality of coal imported in 1934 was generally worse than the previous year, the reason being that the import of Chinese-produced coal has slightly increased (this phenomenon is truly both annoying and gratifying)! The increase and decrease in the import of Chinese coal and Japanese coal are as follows:

| | January to May 1934 | January to May 1933 |

|----------------------|-----------------------|-----------------------|

| Chinese Coal | 1,057,965 tons | 896,167 tons |

| Japanese Coal | 189,343 | 531,933 |

According to the table above, the import of Chinese coal has increased considerably, while the import of Japanese coal has decreased by two-thirds. According to the figures released by the Coal Association, the import tax on domestic coal from January to November increased by 250,000 tons compared with the same period in 1933, while the import of Japanese coal decreased significantly.

However, the above phenomenon is by no means sufficient to indicate the superiority of Chinese coal. On the contrary, it is a manifestation of China's increasing colonialization. Why do we say this? Because the decrease in Japanese coal imports is not due to an increase in Chinese coal production, or an improvement in quality, or a decline in Japanese coal production. The reason lies in the rapid progress of Japan's military supply industry in the past one or two years, which requires a large amount of coal and iron ore. In particular, since the establishment of the Showa Coal Company in early 1933, it has cooperated with the Japanese Industrial Federation to conduct controlled sales of coal. Even the Fushun coal mine in the Northeast (which is, of course, already in the hands of the Japanese) has seen a significant decrease in its imports due to the needs of supplying Japanese and local industries.

| | June to October 1934 | January to October 1933 |

|----------------------|----------------------|-----------------------|

| Chinese Coal | 1,067,700 tons | 862,604 tons |

| Fushun Coal | 169,442 | 266,954 |

Chinese coal from companies such as Datong, Huainan, Kailuan, and Zhongxing is indeed in fierce competition with Japanese coal, which has led to a sharp drop in coal prices. Coal from Japan and the Northeast is indeed difficult to compete with Chinese coal. However, we must note that the so-called Chinese coal at this time is not the product of purely Chinese-owned enterprises. Much of the coal is still produced under the British capital system, and some is even the product of enterprises jointly managed with Japanese capital!

Import Volume of Coal from Various Places from January to October 1934 (Unit: Thousands of Tons)

| Coal Mine Name | Volume | Coal Mine Name | Volume |

|----------------|--------|----------------|--------|

| Zhongxing | 350 | Kailuan | 930 |

| Shandong | 440 | Datong | 30 |

| Hua Dong | 70 | Huainan | 65 |

| Total | 2,140 | | |

The import volume of Kailuan coal accounts for almost half of the total import volume. Generally speaking, since the September 18th Incident, the trend of Chinese people rejecting Japanese goods has been strong, so judging from the import of coal in Shanghai, Chinese coal has indeed increased slightly. Shandong coal imported from Qingdao, Liujiang coal imported from Qinhuangdao, and Shanxi coal imported from Tianjin have all increased. From January to October 1934, the import volume of these coals, nominally called Chinese coal, reached as much as 2.14 million tons. During the same period in 1933, the import volume of these coals was only 1.75 million tons.

Now, let's take a look at the import situation of other foreign coals. Previously, the total annual import of Hongji and Haiphong anthracite coal from Hongji and Haiphong in French-controlled Annam was as high as 300,000 tons. After China implemented a new tariff in May 1933 and increased import taxes, these anthracite coals were greatly reduced. The new tariff implemented on July 1, 1934, increased the import tax on anthracite coal to about six yuan per ton, which had a significant impact on the import of foreign coal. For example, from June to October 1933, their import volume was 35,632 tons, while in the same period in 1934, it suddenly dropped to 18,920 tons.

In summary, although the import of foreign coal in 1934 has decreased, this situation can only indicate that Japan and other countries have drastically increased their demand for coal due to the development of their military and general heavy industries. Generally speaking, this situation should be a favorable condition for the development of China's national coal industry. However, based on the current facts, China's most important mining industry (note that, in terms of the current level of technology, mining is a basic condition for the development of the entire national economy, especially the industrial sector), is mostly in the hands of foreign capital. In recent years, the Kailuan Coal Mine has almost become an arena for British and Japanese capital to compete. Although Britain controls the mining rights, Japan wants to expand its sales of Fushun coal and further wants to encompass the rich resources of the entire North China. It is therefore doing everything possible to destroy it. Secondly, we see the recent active activities of the Japanese in the Shandong Luda and Hanzhi Ping Company aspects, which really make us shudder. They also often send survey teams to Shanxi, Suiyuan, and other places to investigate. In addition to its military significance, this action is at least a strong motivation for the seizure of the rich resources of North China. Looking back at our country's situation, although there is a reorganization of the Zhongyuan Liuhegou mines, the power has fallen into the hands of foreigners, and the results are not good. Other places have also suspended work and reduced work, and all are constantly proceeding. If this continues, China's coal industry will inevitably fall entirely into the hands of foreigners. The increase or decrease in Shanghai's coal import volume in 1934 can only manifest the expansion of foreign coal power in disguise.

Securities

Bond Market Relatively Stable Last Week 243

Last week, from December 24th to 29th, was the last week of December for the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, and also the last week of the 23rd year of the Republic of China. Despite the soaring foreign exchange lending rate, the extreme tightness of credit, and the extreme silver shortage, it was able to pass safely and relatively stably. According to the first two days of the week, Monday and Tuesday, were the last two days of December futures. There was talk in the market that HSBC had shipped back 20 million yuan of silver, and there was some squeezing of shorts and squeezing of longs in the market. However, squeezing shorts was still more common. There were many swap and arbitrage transactions by various groups and retail investors. Because the market price was close to low and far to high, it became increasingly distorted, and all those with active credit were arbitraging, especially in the case of the 96 type, with a monthly interest rate of more than three points being the largest. Therefore, although many deliveries were made in the 16th and 48th types, they were almost defeated by retail investors, and the market price was able to be stable. On Wednesday and Thursday, only one-month futures for January were traded. The foreign exchange lending rate was 4 jiao every day, but people's hearts were not moved by it, and the transaction was very clear, with more people entering the market. The market price had a good face of three or four jiao every day. Friday was the delivery date for December futures. The delivery volume was 40 to 50 million, and the foreign exchange lending rate was as high as 6 jiao, which was the highest price in recent years. This was because the delivery of public bonds required about 30 million yuan temporarily, so it was also temporary in nature. On Saturday, the foreign exchange lending rate was still 5 jiao and 5 fen, which was due to the delivery of cotton cloth and had nothing to do with the influx or outflow. Two-month futures began to enter the market, and there were immediate swap transactions and settlements, because there would be a five-day holiday after this, to avoid the risk, it had to shorten the battle line. Because banks such as the Central Bank and Bank of Communications released 10 million yuan in foreign currency to circulate in the market, people's hearts were at ease, and the market was firm and stable. The transactions of the 23rd year of the Republic of China ended here. According to the year's experience, it should be one of the best years since the September 18th Incident. Since the sudden decline in the Min Affairs at the beginning of the year, the market price has gradually risen. The military reduction has risen from more than 59 yuan to 83 yuan, and the salt tax has risen from more than 45 yuan to more than 64 yuan. The peak was on July 9th, which was the highest price of the year, and also the highest price since the September 18th Incident. The major reasons were the stability of the political situation, the gradual suppression of banditry, and the gradual realization of North-South unity. Moreover, due to the loose and excessive silver credit and the concentration of hot money, although there were unfortunate events such as the emergency of the Japanese-Russian situation, the arrogant statement of Hirota, and the disappearance of Kuramoto, they also rose and fell quickly and did not hurt the overall situation. Since autumn, the outflow of silver has intensified, and the cash reserves in Shanghai have become increasingly depleted. The financial community has sold out month by month, and the foreign exchange lending rate has gradually increased, relying only on retail arbitrage to maintain its stability. Therefore, rumors such as the depreciation of silver coins, inflation, and paper money policies are not facts. The Ministry of Finance has the determination to maintain such a market, and the future is optimistic. At the end of the year, the market price results were mixed, with only a few jiao. The total turnover was 82.472 million yuan.

Exchange Announcement: December 31st is the closing date for all brokers, and the exchange will be closed for one day. January 1st to 3rd, 24th year of the Republic of China, are New Year's holidays, and business will resume as usual from the 4th.

Talking

The General Ledger of Hope 245

— Ge Bai

The calendar has been turned to the last page. From the moment I hung it on the newly wallpapered wall with a ball of hope, and tore it down page by page until today, I feel that the days have passed too quickly. But that ball of hope seems to still be stuck at that time, but when I think about it, it seems too long ago.

The newly delivered calendar is standing upright on the desk with a smile, welcoming me: Happy New Year! Yes, in twenty-four hours, it will be a new beginning. Opening my blank diary, can I still reserve this unfulfilled hope? And who knows what the scene will be when this new set of calendars is turned to the last page?

Humans seem to be forever deceiving themselves. The past is all dead yesterday, and the future is all born today. They put hope in front of them, forever chasing after it, and turn their lives to the last page like a calendar, even leaving it to the next generation to chase after the lamp of hope, just as the old calendar is replaced by the new one, and then torn page by page from the beginning.

I have entrusted my life to hope and can't remember how many sets of calendars I have turned through. On this day every year, I tear off that thin page of the calendar without hesitation, and then happily hang up the new one, as if the hope I have reserved is gradually approaching, and I don't know how much of my life has been wasted!

Looking at the gray wall, this last page is about to become a trace in an instant. Can the new calendar, with a happy New Year smile, competently fulfill the responsibility of this "general ledger"? I am afraid that when it is turned to the last page next year, it will still be an unanswered pending case!

When the Calendar Turns Over 246

— Yingying

Mr. Si sat in front of the raised broken account table, rubbing the impossible-to-blow-away wiping paper, while flipping through the desk calendar placed on the account table! His initial intention seemed to be to count how many calendar pages were left? But just as he touched the shiny chrome-plated desk, which was really like being woven from cotton threads, he suddenly became top-heavy and somersaulted forward. He stared blankly at the supporting legs under the desk for a long time!

He remembered very clearly and accurately. This calendar was specially brought by his son, who worked as a clerk in a large Shanghai bookstore, along with the New Year's goods at the end of last year. Of course, this also cost a lot of money. Not to mention that it is rare in the countryside; even in Shanghai, only large stores and large companies can afford such an exquisite chrome-plated desk calendar, and his son's letter mentioned it several times.

When Mr. Si received this exquisite calendar that he had never seen in his life, he was so happy that he broke a piece of glass on his old glasses, which had been with him for decades.

But he did not regret it. The antique glasses piece, which he had lost for decades, was exchanged for the latest dazzling white copper calendar.

Every day, after getting up, he had to personally turn over the calendar date, as if he had done something proud, and he was happy as if he was!

But recently, Duan Zhen's face has gradually become ugly. Turning the calendar is no longer as happy as before. It seems that this is the work he is most impatient to do; however, if someone else accidentally forgot to turn it over and turned over yesterday's date for him, he would become furious!

It is true that Mr. Si has something important on his mind.

Every day after getting up in the morning and washing, he habitually called for a water pipe, and then many worries formed hundreds of knots on his forehead!

Every day so many people have to eat, but every day no one comes to buy anything. Seeing Wei Fu sitting beside the counter only dozing off, and Chun Gen foolishly looking at the scenery outside like a silly person. In fact, what can Duan Zhen tell them to do? Sometimes it's really hard to bear. After Chun Gen eats, he also nods off. Even if he is forced to get up, he is told to sweep another piece of land.

The counter is piled full of sixteen large palm fans and thirty oiled paper fans that have not been sold for a long time. Except for opium smokers, no one will ever ask about these things.

He also had a time when he thought wishfully that perhaps next summer he would make a great fortune, then he could raise the price, and he could still make money.

The Qian Jingji landlord came to collect the rent six times, and yesterday, when he left, he really rolled his eyes at him for a while.

If you don't pay me back next time, I'm going to seal the door!

He trembled for a long time because of this sentence!

When he got up today, his palms were still trembling so badly. As a result, he lightly turned the calendar, and for no reason it would fall forward.

He will never have a chance to turn over like the calendar!

A Night of Revelry 247

— Qian Hong

The sky hangs low, gray clouds congeal like heavy lead, but snowflakes dance in the air with the north wind. Today, although it is the Christmas of Jesus, wealthy people are celebrating a glorious holiday. However, he had no choice but to brave the snow and wander the streets, begging for his wife and children who were waiting to be fed. He walked back and forth, reaching out in the snow to those noble people coming out of theaters and restaurants, pleading, "Please, do a good deed!" But each time he received only disappointment. When he stepped into his dilapidated home, all he brought back was cold and hunger! He staggered in, stood at the threshold swaying his body, and shook the snowflakes off his clothes. His wife, seeing him, eagerly asked, "Did you get anything?" "No, not even a copper! Alas! Nothing!" He replied wearily and weakly, then went to sit on the edge of the bed. His wife followed, wanting to offer him some comfort in his sorrow. But when her hand touched his shoulder, she couldn't help but cry out: "Oh! You're soaked through!" "Soaked through? It snowed so heavily just now, and it was the time when the theaters were letting out. I stood there for over an hour at the racetrack, thinking I could hail a car for someone and get a few coppers. But what happened? I just stood hungry in the slush, watching people crowding out, happily squeezing into cars and carriages. The snow was falling so hard, I had to dodge the horses' heads and the cars, getting soaked through. All I got was 'Get out of here, you beggar! Get out, get out!' scolding..." He had barely finished speaking when his wife, tears streaming down her face, said to him with sorrow: "You haven't done anything bad, why should people treat you like this..." These words made him roar like a wounded wild animal: "Why should they treat me like this! Have I done anything wrong? The company went bankrupt,

Page 20

I can't find another job, is that my fault? Damn it! Those people either lecture you or curse at you!" "Isn't that right? This morning when I took little Bao Bao out to try to find a solution, the ladies on the street all said, 'You shouldn't bring a child out on such a snowy day!'" This reminded him that when he went out, the innocent child was still crying for food. He turned around and saw that the child was fast asleep. So he thought, the child must be full, right? The moment he thought of this, he felt relieved, as if he had fulfilled his responsibility as a father to raise his child! He forgot the pain he had suffered today, he forgot the cold he felt in his body and the hunger in his stomach. However, he finally asked his wife: "The child must be full, right? What about you?" His wife, who seemed to be lost in thought, was a little puzzled by his question. She replied doubtfully: "What? Full? Where did that come from? Alas! It doesn't matter if we adults go hungry, but this child is so pitiful! From crying with hunger to being exhausted!..." His wife was sobbing. At this moment, the child wrapped in a tattered quilt also woke up, crying that he was hungry and wanted food! The crying made him feel really hungry too. He looked painfully at his wife as she soothed the child, saying "It's not dawn yet, good baby! Go back to sleep, don't cry, daddy brought sausage noodles home yesterday!" This made him think of the good old days, and the miserable life after losing his job. He had thought of committing suicide, but that thought was shattered by his self-esteem. Until today, he was still struggling on the edge of death with his wife and children. He cried out madly: "No, I want to live! I want to live! I want to bring back money and food!" He suddenly left the edge of the bed, ignoring his wife's calls, and rushed out the door again. At this time, the sky was still hanging low, the gray clouds were congealed like heavy lead, and snowflakes were still dancing in the air.

Old Tales for the New Year 248

— Simon

If it weren't for the various decorations and scenes adorning the streets and alleys that made me reluctantly realize that another new year was arriving, this day would have quietly passed by unnoticed. Now I have to put on a smiling face and say to people, as they do to each other, "Happy New Year." In this vulgar sound and smiling face, there is clearly an infinite joy hidden, and the light of infinite hope is shining. But only I am helplessly masking my dark face and pretending to be as happy as everyone else. In fact, all the joys of the world have long been unrelated to me. The eyebrows of others are painted with rare shadows of joy in the New Year, while I have given all of these to sighs and tears.

Passing the so-called New Year with a heart full of sadness.

After wandering outside for many days, my mood and thoughts have been gradually worn away by the complicated affairs of the world to the point of almost losing their function. I remember when I was young, as soon as I heard that the New Year was coming again, I would be so happy that I would jump around all day and couldn't sleep at night, eagerly awaiting the day to come. The New Year was indeed the happiest time for us children, with things to play with and good things to eat. We could do whatever we wanted, and the adults would always listen. Even if we made a big fuss, no one would care. Adults were especially compliant with children's requests at this time.

And on the eve of New Year's Eve, we would gather around the stove with the family to stay up late. These things are ancient history now, and thinking about them only brings about an unspeakable sense of melancholy. Actually, there's no need to trace back to such distant events. Even in the years before I left my hometown, on the eve of the New Year, all I had to do was take a stroll outside in the morning and see fresh red couplets pasted on the doors of every house, and then listen to the sound of firecrackers popping everywhere.

Although I was already standing outside the circle of children setting off firecrackers, being in such a situation would unconsciously cause a scene akin to childhood to surge from my heart.

Now, even this fantasy of the heart is over.

For several years, I have been wandering on the long road of life, feeling the vicissitudes of human affairs and the fleeting nature of life, especially feeling the insignificance of my own life. Squeezed into this sea of people like waves, fierce waves are constantly rolling up, and I know at any time that there is a possibility of being swept into the waves and submerged. Even if not, the boulder of the heavy pressure of real life is enough to knock me down. The burden of life is getting heavier year by year, and it has become heavier than what an ant-like me can bear.

The increase in age is accompanied by the increasing weight of the burden of life. Continuing like this is no different from approaching the edge of the grave day by day.

The New Year has come, and my feet are softened again by the sudden increase in weight on my back, and my eyes are blurred.

Moon Overhead Night 249

— Hui Ren

Because I often hear people reciting the line, "How many times in life do you see the moon overhead!" the poem aroused my determination to wait for tonight.

Usually, when I wander alone in the moonlight, I always see my shadow cast in front of or behind me, which looks very lonely. Because of this, I become sad alone, either thinking about home or lamenting my own fate. Except for a poet or someone who already has a companion, most people will feel a little sentimental about the moonlit night! Because it is strangely gloomy and doesn't give people any warmth. In the past, some people used silver-gray...sentences to describe or symbolize their environment, which can also prove people's reflection on the moonlit night scene.

As for the moon overhead night being very close to the arrival of the New Year, this seems to give people a stimulus, telling people not to let themselves fall into depression again, and should start a new life in another new year. It hides your shadow, which is equal to telling you to forget the past.

After finishing dinner today, I am preparing for how to enjoy it. As for cigarettes, coffee, tea, etc., they have already been planned. Watching the clock tick by minute by minute, watching the moon move eastward little by little, I feel as happy as if a happy event is coming.

Tonight the frost is very heavy and the wind is blowing very hard. Looking at the clouds in the sky, they are also very dense and heavy. The moon is constantly being swallowed and spit out by the clouds, which makes me worry. Will I not be able to see the moonlight at midnight? The time spent is a small matter, but the disappointment afterwards is a bit...

Time is sinking moment by moment, and the environment is becoming silent little by little. The sound of footsteps on the street can be clearly counted. I thought that there would be no one active on the street anymore, but strangely, almost every half hour a team of heavy leather shoes would pass from the street, loudly singing songs in their mouths. Later I learned that it was the night patrol team of Japanese soldiers.

This seems to be a great stimulus. It ruined my moon viewing tonight, and it destroyed the happiness in my heart! Because it brought me some inevitable awareness problems, almost touching my heart like a thorn, especially when the sound of their leather shoes approached the park.

Finally, I know that sadness is not simple, personal, but complex, everyone's; that is, the moon overhead cannot illuminate its own tail, showing its own sadness, but similarly, others will come.

As a result, there was no moonlight at all at midnight, but the electric lights on the road cast my shadow, which was strangely long, on the ground.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Special

Appreciating a Confidante: Kinnie Raymons Accepts an Engagement with RKO 255

— Su Hua

The more profound the stimulation one receives, the longer the impression remains in the mind. This is a very common law of memory. Do we still remember her? That innocent and lively "Sweetheart" – Nancy Carroll. What a deep impression she left on us! Although it has been many years since she starred in "Youth Club" ("Follow Thru"), I'm afraid most of us haven't forgotten it. In recent years, she seems to have become somewhat distant from us, and we haven't seen her films. The apple-like face and those two charming dimples have been longed for by many. This is because she has left Hollywood for several years, left the hustle and bustle of the film set, avoided the glaring mercury lights, and gone to Europe to enjoy a somewhat leisurely life. Before she left Hollywood, she actually co-starred in a film with the now-famous Kinnie Raymons. At that time, Kinnie Raymons was just a new actor on the silver screen, and that film co-starring with Nancy Carroll was his first appearance on the screen. Although that film was not produced in Hollywood, his performance at that time was recognized by Hollywood production companies. They immediately invited him to the studio. Over the years, he has worked tirelessly, coupled with his innate talent; his art has been steadily improving, and he has now become an important figure in leading male roles. Isn't his success in "The Great Waltz" ironclad proof? Kinnie Raymons was born with a talent for acting. He played child roles at the age of five, and later he even left his original school to study at a drama school. After graduating, he lived his stage life. On the talent-rich Broadway stage in New York, his theatrical talent and his youthful handsomeness had already gained him considerable recognition and special attention. Sylvia Sidney, the leading actress in "Madame Butterfly," had already collaborated with him on stage and achieved success. Now both of them hold high positions on the Hollywood star throne.

In addition to being a talented actor, Kinnie Raymons is also an all-around athlete. He can ride horses, swim, box, fence, and also play tennis and golf very well. Haven't we already admired his good piano playing in "The Great Waltz"?

Of course, he is now praised by the world in Hollywood, and he should be extremely grateful to Nancy Carroll for his first collaboration with her. After Nancy Carroll returned to Hollywood and finished filming "Springtime for Henry" for Fox, RKO hired her with a large sum of money to star in the million-dollar epic film "Transatlantic Merry-Go-Round," which had been in preparation for many years. With the "Sweetheart" starring in this epic film, the female lead was of course not a problem. It was just the selection of the male lead that troubled the authorities at RKO. Of course, they all knew that Kinnie Raymons was the most suitable talent for this film, but Kinnie Raymons was a very famous and popular star who was not bound by contracts, and everyone was vying to hire him, fearing that he would not be able to spare the time. Later, the company felt that it would be difficult to succeed unless Nancy Carroll went to discuss it with him. Of course, Nancy Carroll was the helper of his success, and he would definitely not refuse. So, as soon as she came, he immediately rejected the contracts of other companies and agreed to her. The "Transatlantic Merry-Go-Round," which is about to be released locally, was finally completed after RKO exhausted its personnel, effort, and money. Kinnie Raymons' spirit of appreciating a confidante is of course admirable; and how could our "Sweetheart" not be moved by it? (The End)

Film Review

Review of "The Merry Widow" 256

— Ling He

| Nanjing |

I remember when sound films were just maturing, "The Love Parade," starring Maurice Chevalier and Jeanette MacDonald, caused a sensation in Shanghai. That film was not only a large-scale musical, but also in color, which gave the audience great satisfaction. At the same time, the names of Maurice Chevalier and Jeanette MacDonald became known to everyone, young and old, and the songs from "The Love Parade" became household names. That kind of grand occasion is something that people will not forget.

Based on this alone, one can determine the box office success of "The Merry Widow." It is also starring the leading actors of "The Love Parade," and the audience of Maurice Chevalier and Jeanette MacDonald will naturally not easily let go of this opportunity to enjoy it. As for the silent film "The Merry Widow," its influence on the audience is naturally also very great.

In addition, we might as well further explore the reasons for the box office success of this film. It is very clear that the fantasy of the story gives people beautiful dreams. That handsome and dashing count, that beautiful and affectionate wealthy widow, in such a luxurious and extravagant environment, with a happy ending, the structure of such a story is similar to the Chinese stories of talented scholars and beautiful women that people welcome. Especially at present, in the midst of the cruel reality that gives people very unpleasant situations, this film is even more sufficient to give noble people a wonderful comfort, although this comfort is very empty. As for some viewers, they are also very familiar with the name of the director Ernst Lubitsch, which may not be one of the reasons for the box office success.

Now, let's examine Lubitsch's style. From "The Love Parade" to "The Merry Widow," his style has not changed. His stories are certainly far from reality, and in the completely fantasy plot, what he needs are grand scenes, luxurious props, and gorgeous costumes. Thus, talented men and beautiful women, in the joys and sorrows of the plot, in the beautiful songs, in the graceful dance troupes, he grasps the charming scenery, the romantic atmosphere, and the gentle affection, which are all so-called bright and harmonious styles. In short, he should be a typical capitalist film artist, and this "The Merry Widow" and the like are naturally outstanding works of capitalist films.

In terms of the old-fashioned expression methods of film art, people cannot find so-called flaws in "The Merry Widow." Everything seems smooth and brilliant, whether it is the gentle dialogue, the intoxicating music, or the frivolous movements, under the appropriate weaving and tempo, everything is a top-notch expression of capitalism. Of course, it should be mentioned here that the screenwriters Enrest Vajda and Sarnson Raphaelsono handled the rhythm of the play very smoothly, and Franz Lehar's composition also helped the film to achieve success. As for Jeanette MacDonald's acting skills, when she kissed his hand, her subtle expression of her inner feelings and desires in silence, just this point alone can prove her experience. As for Maurice Chevalier and the actor who played the ambassador, they both performed extremely well.

Review of "The Pearl Necklace" 257

— You Jing

| Carlton Cinema Screening |

Bao Tianxiao's novel "Empty Valley Orchid" was praised by most readers at the time. After the Star Film Company made it into a film, due to Zhang Zhiyun's considerable success in acting, it even more widely appealed to many audiences at that time.

The reason why the novel "Empty Valley Orchid" was able to "cause a sensation" was not accidental, but because it used some emerging facts at the time, such as trains, photography, medicine, female teachers in schools, patriotic wars, and freedom of marriage, to quite successfully express the general new tragicomedies in society at that time, and ethically and emotionally explored the old conflicts of love and jealousy. At that time, this relatively new creative attitude and method was indeed more accepted and welcomed by the general emerging classes at that time.

With the full-dialogue sound film "The Pearl Necklace," which only appeared on the scene at the end of 1934, we should give it a new evaluation because of its new posture. But it is a bit regrettable that this new "The Pearl Necklace," compared to "Empty Valley Orchid," does not seem to give the audience anything more or better, except for replacing part of the subtitles with dialogue. If I am not too demanding, some of the deeper and more touching parts in the silent film do not seem to have the same effect here as before.

Looking at the entire film, the author seems to be a little weaker in his skills, somewhat constrained by the story, and only using the pictures to explain, without enriching and deeply portraying what is necessary. In other words, the transition scenes are done well, but many places that serve as the center and climax of this script also pass by flatly. A play based on ethics, which should have a full emotional expression, lost its due effect due to the inadequate handling of the atmosphere in the picture. Some shots are simply a waste, and dialogue was not used to save unnecessary scenes. For example, in the picture, Lan Xun rode his horse for a long way, and then Zhu ran to tell her father, "Brother is here," and then there is a section of Lan Xun riding his horse before they meet. Zhu said to Lan Xun, "I'll go tell my dad," pointing to "That's my dad," and then a long piece of film is shown, they meet, and Lan Xun asks again about "your name," etc. At the wedding banquet, the picture has already shown many seats, and then Lan Xun comes to invite the guests out, repeating a piece of the seats that had been shown. After the child is sick, since Mrs. Lan was called by telephone, it is not necessary to use the picture to repeat the doctor's words, and Lan Xun had already called her on the screen, and You Lan still makes many trivial expressions, and in the telephone, she also repeats the scene of the doctor seeing the child with dialogue. It is not necessary to call the roll a second time for a mother who is also a teacher to know that a child is absent due to illness, as it is not needed to be explained. Because dialogue and pictures cannot be used to complement each other, the randomness and repetition make the whole film scattered and loose, reducing the power of the play.

Language, as the main part of a sound film, is the defining significance of a sound film, but the speech in "The Pearl Necklace" feels too unreal. The stage language of Chinese sound films did not start with "The Pearl Necklace." The language in the first half of "Song of China" is also too artificial and exaggerated. We know that on the stage, in order to make more audiences hear clearly, it is necessary to be more artificial and exaggerated than usual, but sound films have the effect of loudspeakers, so being artificial and exaggerated is not only unnatural, but also harmful. In addition to the artificial and exaggerated tone in "The Pearl Necklace," the dialogue in the section about hiring a maid is also as sharp as that of a Beijing opera Dan (female) role.

Makeup is also not well applied here. In addition to some people not using makeup to help with expressions, Fan Xuepeng's eye makeup looks worse than swollen when looking down.

The voice and face of the child who plays Liang Yan's child are not suitable. I think using a more pretty and lively person to play the role would better show the character's pity and loveliness in the play, in order to increase the effect of the play.

Among the actors, Ye Qiuxin and Wei Pengfei are better. Fan Xuepeng may not be very suitable for acting in this kind of play, so she is just average.

"The Pearl Necklace" Premieres at the Carlton Cinema 258

— Bai Yun

"Empty Valley Orchid" is a popular and well-known novel. Before, there were only silent films, but now Tianyi Company has made it into a sound film, renamed "The Pearl Necklace," co-directed by Shao Zuiweng and Gao Lihen, starring Fan Xuepeng, Ye Qiuxin, Chen Qiufeng, Wei Pengfei, and more than a dozen other major stars. The plot is full of joys and sorrows and is very moving. There are several specially made new songs in the film, such as Gao Tianqi's "Hypnotic Song" and Ren Guang and An E's collaboration "Wishing My Brother Returns," with very melodious notes. The exquisite scenery and costumes, and the clarity of the light and sound, surpass all other films. The film has been officially screened at the Carlton Theatre since the 30th of this month.

Film Novel

Nursing Escapades (The White Parade) 259

(Part 1)

— Su Yin

Lasky-Fox Production, Starring John Boles, Loretta Young, etc.

Mitchell Lee Hospital has newly recruited seventy-five nurses, including Joan, Zita, Brandy, Codylo, and Vicki. Joan is intelligent and beautiful, and is obviously the best among them. She chose the shy Zita as her roommate, and Brandy and Codylo also grouped together. Zita, newly entered the hospital, found the work too heavy and felt overwhelmed, and missed her lover in her hometown, and was depressed all day long. In order to comfort Zita, Joan said that she also had a lover, and that lover was none other than the nationally renowned polo champion, the wealthy young man Lonar Wahl III. Because when they were talking, they were flipping through a newspaper, and Lonar's photo happened to be revealed in front of them, so Joan made it up. Unexpectedly, Zita actually believed it. Later, when a group of new nurses ran to a nearby pharmacy to eat ice cream and malted milk, Zita told everyone what Joan had said. Everyone who heard it also believed it, except for Codylo, who was self-confident and did not believe that Joan was Lonar Wahl III's sweetheart. She openly expressed that she did not believe it, so she argued with Brandy, and neither would give in. So the two of them made a bet. Codylo immediately wrote a letter to Lonar Wahl, asking him to clearly answer whether he and Joan had a marriage contract. Lonar Wahl received Codylo's letter and knew that someone was pretending to be his fiancée, and was very angry, but his secretary was very discreet. He replied to Codylo on behalf of Lonar, and did not deny the marriage contract between Lonar Wahl and Joan. In this way, Codylo lost the bet, and in a fit of anger, Codylo focused on taking the opportunity to retaliate against Joan. Sure enough, when Joan was practicing being a patient, Codylo tried to harm her, but the director of the nursing class, the fat Sarah, saved her.

When the six-month trial period was over, several of the original ten first-class nurses were removed from their positions after being singled out. But one of them, a Southern woman named Anna, usually did not study hard and did not worry, but when the time came, she actually passed and was retained. Later, Joan actually became acquainted with Lonar Wahl III. As it happened, the newspaper that day prominently published that Lonar Wahl was coming. In order to prove whether Joan and Lonar had a marriage contract, Codylo specially brought several companions to Central Station to see if Joan would come. Joan really came. Just as Lonar Wahl got off the train and was about to step into the car, Joan rushed up, pushed Lonar into the car, jumped in herself, and quickly ordered the car to drive away. In the car, Joan shyly apologized to Lonar, telling him the reason why she had to do so under the pressure of her companions. Only then did Lonar remember the letter he had received before, and realized that the person who was pretending to be his fiancée was this person. But Joan was so beautiful, and now being in the same car with her, he couldn't help but fall in love at first sight, and was very lucky. He not only agreed to Joan's request to temporarily save face for her, but also went all the way to the West, and actually accompanied Joan to the pharmacy near the hospital. The nurses there all gathered around to see Joan's fiancé. Joan introduced them one by one. Lonar even gave each of them a big bag of candy. So Codylo had nothing to say. However, things in the world turn out to be true, and before he left that place, he had indeed fallen into the abyss of love with Joan. (To be continued)
